\v	24	Naizvozvo Jehovha wakanditsivira zvichienderana nekururama kwangu, zvichienderana nekuchena kwemaoko angu pamberi pemeso ake.
\p
\v	25	Kune ane tsitsi munozviratidza mune tsitsi; kune munhu wakarurama munozviratidza makarurama;
\v	26	kune wakachena munozviratidza makachena; uye kune wakatsauka munozviratidza makatsauka.
\v	27	Nokuti imwi muchaponesa vanhu vanotambudzwa; asi muchaderedza meso ekuzvikudza.
\v	28	Nokuti imwi muchatungidza mwenje wangu; Jehovha Mwari wangu achavhenekera rima rangu.
\v	29	Nokuti nemwi ndakamhanya  nemuhondo; uye naMwari wangu ndichakwakuka rusvingo.
\p
\v	30	Mwari, nzira yake yakaperera; shoko raJehovha rakaedzwa; inhovo kune vose vanovimba naye.
\v	31	Nokuti ndiani Mwari, kunze kwaJehovha? Uye ndiani dombo, kusara kwaMwari wedu?
\v	32	NdiMwari anondisunga chiuno nesimba, nekuperedzera nzira yangu.
\v	33	Anoita tsoka dzangu dzive sedzenondokadzi, nekundiisa panzvimbo dzangu dzakakwirira.
\v	34	Anodzidzisira maoko angu hondo, kuti uta hwendarira huhwemburwe nemaoko angu.
\v	35	Makandipawo nhovo yeruponeso rwenyu; neruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwakanditsigira, uye unyoro hwenyu hunondikudza.
\v	36	Makafaranukisa nhanho yangu pasi pangu, kuti zvidodoma zvangu zvisatedzemuka.
\p
\v	37	Ndakadzingirira vavengi vangu, ndokuvabata, uye handina kudzokera shure kusvika vapedzwa.
\v	38	Ndakavapwanya, kusvika vakonewa kumuka; vakawa pasi petsoka dzangu.
\v	39	Nokuti makandisungira chiuno hondo nesimba; makaisa pasi pangu vanondimukira.
\v	40	Makandipawo mutsipa wevavengi vangu; avo vanondivenga ndakavaparadza.
\v	41	Vakachema asi pasina muponesi, kuna Jehovha, asi haana kuvapindura.
\v	42	Zvino ndakavakuya seguruva pamberi pemhepo; ndakavadurura sematope enzira dzemumusha.
\p
\v	43	Makandinunura pakukakavadzana kwevanhu; makandimisa kuva musoro wendudzi; vanhu vandisina kuziva vachandishandira.
\v	44	Pakunzwa kwenzeve vachanditeerera; vatorwa vachazvininipisa kwandiri neunyepedzeri.
\v	45	Vatorwa vachasvava, vagobuda munhare dzavo vachidedera.
\p
\v	46	Jehovha mupenyu; uye dombo rangu ngariropafadzwe; uye Mwari weruponeso rwangu ngaarumbidzwe.
\v	47	Mwari anondipa kutsiva kuzhinji; uye anowisira vechirudzi pasi pangu.
\v	48	Wakandinunura pavavengi vangu; hongu, imwi makandisimudza pamusoro peavo vanondimukira; makandinunura pamunhu ane chisimba.
\v	49	Naizvozvo ndichakuvongai, Jehovha, pakati pevechirudzi, uye ndichaimbira zita renyu rumbidzo.
\v	50	Anokurisa rudzikunuro rukuru rwamambo wake, anoitira muzodzwa wake tsitsi, kuna Dhavhidhi, nekumbeu yake kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\c	19
\s	Mabasa aMwari nemirairo yake
\p
\v	1	Matengaanorondedzera kubwinya kwaMwari; uye muchadenga munoparidza basa remaoko ake.
\v	2	Zuvarinodururira nhauro kuzuva, neusiku hunoratidza ruzivo kuusiku.
\v	3	Hapananhauro uye hapana mashoko inzwi razvo parisina kunzwikwa.
\v	4	Rwonzirwazvo rwakabudira panyika yose, nemashoko azvo kumugumo wenyika. Wakamisira zuva tende mazviri.
\v	5	Uyeiro rakaita sechikomba chinobuda mukamuri macho; rinofara semhare kumhanya  panzira.
\v	6	Kubudakwaro kunobva pamugumo wematenga, nekupoteredza kwaro kusvika kumigumo yaro; uye hakuna chakavanzirwa kupisa kwaro.
\p
\v	7	MurauwaJehovha wakaperera, unoshandura mweya weupenyu; chipupuro chaJehovha ichokwadi, chinochenjedza asina mano.
\v	8	ZvimisozvaJehovha zvakarurama, zvinofadza moyo; murairo waJehovha wakachena, unovhenekera maziso.
\v	9	KutyaJehovha kwakachena, kunogara nekusingaperi; mitongo yaJehovha ichokwadi, yakarurama zvakazara.
\v	10	Zvinoshuvika kupfuura goridhe, hongu, kupfuura goridhe zhinji rakaisvonaka; zvinotapirawo kupfuura uchi, nemusvi wemazinga euchi.
\v	11	Uye muranda wenyu anonyeverwa nazvo; pakuzvichengeta pane mubairo mukuru.
\v	12	Ndiani anganzwisisa zvitadzo? Ndichenesei  pamhosva pane zvakavanda.
\v	13	Chengetai muranda wenyu kubva pakuzvikudzawo; ngavarege kutonga pamusoro pangu. Ipapo ndichava wakakwana ndive wakachena pachitadzo chikuru.
\p
\v	14	Mashoko emuromo wangu nemurangariro wemoyo wangu ngazvigamuchirike pamberi penyu, Jehovha, dombo rangu nemudzikunuri wangu.
\c	2
\s	Kutonga kwemuzodzwa waJehovha
\p
\v	1	Seindudzi dzichiita bope, nevanhu vachifunganya zvisina maturo?
\v	2	Madzimamboenyika akazvimisa, nevatungamiriri vanoita rangano pamwe chete, kurwisa Jehovha nekurwisa muzodzwa wake,  vachiti:
\v	3	Ngatidamburezvisungo zvavo, uye tirase makashu avo kubva kwatiri.
\v	4	Iyeagere kumatenga achaseka; Ishe achavasveveredza.
\v	5	Ipapoachataura kwavari mukutsamwa kwake, nekuvavhundusa nehasha dzake.
\v	6	Zvakadaroini ndakagadza mambo wangu pamusoro peZiyoni, gomo reutsvene hwangu.
\p
\v	7	Ndicharondedzeramaererano nechimiso: Jehovha wakati kwandiri: Iwe uri mwanakomana wangu, nhasi ini ndakubereka.
\v	8	Kumbirakwandiri, zvino ndichapa vechirudzi  vave nhaka yako, nemigumo yenyika  ive yako.
\v	9	Muchavaguranetsvimbo yesimbi; muchavapwanya sehari yemuumbi.
\v	10	Naizvozvo ikozvino chenjerai, imwi madzimambo; murairike, imwi vatongi venyika.
\v	11	Shumirai Jehovha nekutya, uye farai nekudedera.
\v	12	Tsvodai mwanakomana, zvimwe angatsamwa, mugoparara  panzira, kana hasha dzake dzopfuta hadzo zvishoma. Vakaropafadzwa vose vanovimba naye.
\c	20
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kukunda
\p
\v	1	Jehovhangaakupindure pazuva redambudziko; zita raMwari waJakove ngarikukwiridzire.
\v	2	Ngaakutumirerubatsiro runobva panzvimbo tsvene; uye akutsigire ari paZiyoni.
\v	3	Ngaarangarirezvipo zvako zvose, uye agamuchire chipo chako chinopiswa. Sera.
\v	4	Ngaakupezvinoenderana nemoyo wako, agozadzisa zano rako rose.
\v	5	Tichadananemufaro muruponeso rwako; nemuzita raMwari wedu tichasimudza mureza. Jehovha ngaazadzise mikumbiro yako yose.
\p
\v	6	Zvinondinoziva kuti Jehovha anoponesa muzodzwa wake; achamupindura ari kumatenga ake matsvene, nemasimba eruponeso rweruoko rwake rwerudyi.
\v	7	Vamwe vanovimba nengoro, uye vamwe nemabhiza; asi isu ticharangarira zita raJehovha Mwari wedu.
\v	8	Ivovakotamiswa, vawa; asi isu tasimuka, uye takamira.
\v	9	Ponesai,Jehovha; mambo ngaatipindure pazuva rekudana kwedu.
\c	21
\s	Kuvonga Mwari pakununurwa
\p
\v	1	Mamboachafara musimba renyu, Jehovha; nemuruponeso rwenyu achafara zvikuru sei!
\v	2	Makamupachishuvo chemoyo wake, uye hamuna kunyima chikumbiro chemiromo yake. Sera.
\v	3	Nokutimunomuchingura nemaropafadzo ezvakanaka; munodzika korona yegoridhe rakaisvonaka pamusoro wake.
\v	4	Wakakumbiraupenyu kwamuri; mukamupa ihwo; urefu hwemazuva nekusingaperi narinhi.
\v	5	Rukudzorwake rukuru paruponeso rwenyu; kubwinya nekukudzwa makaisa pamusoro pake.
\v	6	Nokutimakamuita wakaropafadzwa kwazvo nekusingaperi; makamupembedza nemufaro pakuvapo kwenyu.
\v	7	Nokutimambo anovimba naJehovha, uye netsitsi dzeWekumusoro-soro haangazungunuswi.
\p
\v	8	Ruokorwenyu rwuchawana vavengi venyu vose; ruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwuchawana avo vanokuvengai.
\v	9	Muchavaitavave sevira remoto panguva yekuvapo kwenyu. Jehovha achavamedza pakutsamwa kwake, uye moto uchavapedza.
\v	10	Chibereko chavo muchaparadza kubva panyika, nembeu yavo kubva pakati pevana vevanhu.
\v	11	Nokuti vakatandavadzira zvakaipa kukurwisai; vakaronga zano rakaipa; vachakundikana.
\v	12	Nokuti muchavafuratisa; nehungiso dzenyu dzeuta muchagadzira  miseve kurwisa chiso chavo.
\p
\v	13	Simukai Jehovha, pasimba renyu; tichaimba nekuitira mumhanzi simba renyu.
\c	22
\s	Kuchema kwemunhu wakasiiwa naMwari
\p
\v	1	Mwariwangu, Mwari wangu, mandisiireiko? Muri kure nekundibatsira,  nepamashoko ekuvovora kwangu?
\v	2	Mwariwangu, ndinodana masikati, asi hamupinduri; nepausiku, asi handina kunyarara.
\v	3	Asiimwi muri mutsvene, mugere  parumbidzo dzaIsraeri.
\v	4	Madzibabaedu akavimba nemwi; vakavimba, imwi ndokuvanunura.
\v	5	Vakachemakwamuri, ndokununurwa; vakavimba nemwi, uye havana kunyadziswa.
\v	6	Asiini ndiri honye, uye handisi munhu, chizvidziwa chevanhu, nechinoshorwa nevanhu.
\v	7	Vosevanondiona vanondiseka, vanoshamisa muromo, vanodzungudza musoro,  vachiti:
\v	8	Zviiseikuna Jehovha; ngaamununure; ngaamurwire, nokuti anomufarira.
\p
\v	9	Asindimwi makandibudisa muchizvaro; makandivimbisa  ndichiri pamazamu amai vangu.
\v	10	Ndakarasirwa kwamuri kubva pachizvaro; imwi muri Mwari wangu kubva padumbu ramai vangu.
\v	11	Regai kuva kure neni; nokuti dambudziko riri pedo; nokuti hapana mubatsiri.
\v	12	Hando zhinji dzakandikomba; dzakasimba dzeBhashani dzakandikomberedza.
\v	13	Dzinondishamisira muromo wadzo, shumba inobvamburanya uye inoomba.
\v	14	Ndakadururwa semvura, nemapfupa angu ose aparadzana; moyo wangu wakaita senamo; wakanyauka mukati meura hwangu.
\v	15	Simba rangu rakaoma sechaenga; nerurimi rwangu rwakanamatira pashaya dzangu; uye makandiisa paguruva rerufu.
\v	16	Nokuti imbwa dzakandikomberedza; ungano yevakaipa yakandipoteredza; vakaboora maoko angu nemakumbo angu.
\v	17	Ndingaverenga mapfupa angu ose; ivo vanonditarisa, vanondinan'anidza.
\v	18	Vanogovana nguvo dzangu pakati pavo, nekukanda mujenya pamusoro pechipfeko changu.
\p
\v	19	Asi imwi Jehovha, regai kuva kure; simba rangu, kurumidzai kurubatsiro rwangu.
\v	20	Nunurai mweya weupenyu wangu pamunondo; iwo woga wangu pasimba rembwa.
\v	21	Ndiponesei pamuromo weshumba; nokuti makandipindura ndiri panyanga dzenyati.
\p
\v	22	Ndicharondedzera zita renyu kuhama dzangu; ndichakurumbidzai pakati peungano.
\v	23	Imwi munotya Jehovha, murumbidzei; imwi mose chizvarwa chaJakove, mukudzei; uye mumutyei, imwi mose chizvarwa chaIsraeri.
\v	24	Nokuti haana kuzvidza kana kusema dambudziko reanotambudzwa, uye haana kumuvanzira chiso chake; asi paakachema kwaari, wakanzwa.
\v	25	Rumbidzo yangu nekuda kwenyu ichava paungano huru; ndicharipa mhiko dzangu pamberi pevanomutya.
\v	26	Vanyoro vachadya ndokuguta; vacharumbidza Jehovha ivo vanomutsvaka; moyo wenyu uchararama nekusingaperi.
\v	27	Migumo yose yenyika icharangarira ndokudzokera kuna Jehovha; nemarudzi ose evahedheni achashumira pamberi penyu.
\v	28	Nokuti ushe ndehwaJehovha; uye anotonga pakati pevahedheni.
\v	29	Vakakora vose venyika vachadya uye vachashumira; vose vanoburukira kuguruva vachafugama pamberi pake, neasina kuchengeta mweya weupenyu wake uri mupenyu.
\v	30	Mbeu ichamushumira; icharondedzerwa kuna Ishe kuzera iro.
\v	31	Vachauya uye vachadudzira kururama kwake kuvanhu vachazozvarwa, kuti wakazviita.
\c	23
\s	Jehovha mufudzi wangu
\p
\v	1	Jehovhamufudzi wangu; handishaiwi.
\v	2	Anondirarisapamafuro manyoro; anondisesedza pamvura inozorodza.
\v	3	Anovandudzamweya weupenyu wangu; anondisesedza panzira dzekururama nekuda kwezita rake.
\v	4	Hongu,kunyange ndikafamba nemumupata wemumvuri werufu, handingatyi chakaipa, nokuti imwi muneni; tsvimbo yenyu nemudonzvo wenyu, ndizvo zvinondinyaradza.
\v	5	Munogadziratafura mberi kwangu pamberi pevavengi vangu; munozodza musoro wangu nemafuta; mukombe wangu unopfachuka.
\v	6	Zvirokwazvokunaka nenyasha zvichanditevera mazuva ose eupenyu hwangu; uye ndichagara mumba maJehovha kusvika paurefu hwemazuva.
\c	24
\s	Jehovha weumambo
\p
\v	1	NyikandeyaJehovha, nekuzara kwayo, nyika nevagere mairi.
\v	2	Nokutiiye wakaiteya pamusoro pemakungwa, nekuisimbisa pamusoro penzizi.
\v	3	Ndianiachakwira mugomo raJehovha? Kana ndiani achamira panzvimbo yake tsvene?
\v	4	Uyoane maoko akachena nemoyo wakashambidzika; asingasimudziri mweya weupenyu wake kune zvisina maturo, neasingapiki mukunyengera.
\v	5	Iyeachagamuchira maropafadzo kubva kuna Jehovha, nekururamiswa kubva kuna Mwari weruponeso rwake.
\v	6	Urwurudzi rweavo vanomutsvaka, vanotsvaka chiso chenyu,  iye Jakove. Sera.
\p
\v	7	Simudzaimisoro yenyu, imwi masuwo; uye simudzwai, imwi magonhi arinhi narinhi; kuti kupinde mambo wekubwinya.
\v	8	Ndianiuyu mambo wekubwinya? Jehovha ane simba neumhare, Jehovha ane umhare pahondo.
\v	9	Simudzaimisoro yenyu imwi masuwo; hongu simukai imwi magonhi arinhi narinhi; kuti kupinde mambo wekubwinya.
\v	10	Ndiani uyu mambo wekubwinya? Jehovha wehondo, ndiye mambo wekubwinya. Sera.
\c	25
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kutungamirirwa, kangamwiro nekuchengetedzwa
\p
\v	1	KwamuriJehovha, ndinosimudzira mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	2	Mwariwangu, ndinovimba nemwi, ngandirege kunyadziswa; vavengi vangu ngavarege kupemberera pamusoro pangu.
\v	3	Hongu,kusanyadziswa umwe wevanokumirira; ngavanyadziswe vanodarika pasina chikonzero.
\v	4	Ndiratidzeinzira dzenyu, Jehovha; ndidzidzisei makwara enyu.
\v	5	Nditungamirireimuchokwadi yenyu, uye ndidzidzisei; nokuti imwi muri Mwari weruponeso rwangu; ndakakumirirai zuva rose.
\v	6	Rangarirai,Jehovha, nyasha dzenyu neunyoro hwenyu, nokuti zvai vapo kubva rinhi narinhi.
\v	7	Regaikurangarira zvivi zveudiki hwangu, nezvitadzo zvangu; zvichienderana nengoni dzenyu imwi mundirangarire, nekuda kwekunaka kwenyu, Jehovha.
\p
\v	8	Jehovhawakanaka uye wakarurama; naizvozvo achadzidzisa vatadzi panzira.
\v	9	Achatungamiriravanyoro pamutongo, nekudzidzisa vanyoro nzira yake.
\v	10	Nzira dzose dzaJehovha unyoro nechokwadi kune avo vanochengeta sungano yake nezvipupuriro zvake.
\v	11	Nekuda kwezita renyu, Jehovha, kanganwirai chitadzo changu, nokuti chikuru.
\v	12	Ndeupi munhu anotya Jehovha? Achamudzidzisa nenzira  yaachasarudza.
\v	13	Mweya weupenyu wake uchagara muzvakanaka; uye mbeu yake ichagara nhaka yenyika.
\v	14	Zvakavanzika zvaJehovha ndezvevanomutya; nesungano yake k uizivisa kwavari.
\v	15	Meso angu anorambira pana Jehovha, nokuti ndiye achabudisa tsoka dzangu pamumbure.
\p
\v	16	Tendeukirai kwandiri, mugondinzwira ngoni, nokuti ndiri ndoga, ndinotambudzika.
\v	17	Matambudziko emoyo wangu akura; ndibudisei panjodzi dzangu.
\v	18	Tarisai dambudziko rangu, nekurwadziwa kwangu; uye kanganwirai zvivi zvangu zvose.
\v	19	Tarisai vavengi vangu nokuti vakawanda; uye vanondivenga nehasha dzembengo.
\v	20	Chengetai mweya weupenyu wangu, mundinunure; ngandirege kunyadziswa, nokuti ndinovimba nemwi.
\v	21	Uchokwadi nekururama ngazvindichengete, nokuti ndinokumirirai.
\p
\v	22	Mwari, dzikinurai Israeri kubva panjodzi dzake dzose.
\c	26
\s	Munhu asina mhosva anonyengeterera kururamisirwa
\p
\v	1	NditongereiJehovha, nokuti ini ndakafamba muuchokwadi hwangu; ndakavimbawo naJehovha; handitedzemuki.
\v	2	NdinzvereiJehovha, mugondiedza; natsurudzai itsvo dzangu nemoyo wangu.
\v	3	Nokutiunyoro hwenyu huri pamberi pemeso angu, uye ndakafamba muchokwadi chenyu.
\p
\v	4	Handinakugara nevanhu vekunyengera, uye handingafambi nevanovanza.
\v	5	Ndakavengaungano yevaiti vezvakaipa, uye handigari nevatadzi.
\v	6	Ndichashambidzamaoko angu mukusava nemhosva; ndigopoteredza aritari yenyu, Jehovha.
\v	7	Kutindinzwise nenzwi rekuvonga, uye ndirondedzere mabasa enyu ose anoshamisa.
\v	8	Jehovha,ndakada ugaro hweimba yenyu, nenzvimbo yetabhenakeri yekubwinya kwenyu.
\v	9	Musaunganidzamweya weupenyu wangu pamwe nevatadzi, neupenyu hwangu pamwe nevarume veropa.
\v	10	Mumaoko avo mune uipi, neruoko rwavo rwerudyi rwuzere fufuro.
\v	11	Asi ini ndichafamba muuchokwadi hwangu; ndidzikunurei, mundinzwire tsitsi.
\v	12	Rutsoka rwangu rwakamira panzvimbo yakaenzana; ndicharumbidza Jehovha padziungano.
\c	27
\s	Jehovha ndiye chiedza neruponeso
\p
\v	1	Jehovhachiedza changu neruponeso rwangu; ndiani wandingatya? Jehovha isimba reupenyu hwangu; ndiani wandingabvunda?
\v	2	Pakaswederakwandiri vakaipa, vavengi vangu, nevadzivisi vangu kwandiri, kuzodya nyama yangu, ivo vakagumburwa vakawa.
\v	3	Kunyangehondo ikandidzikira musasa, moyo wangu haungatyi; kunyange kurwa kukandimukira, ndichavimba neizvi.
\v	4	Chinhuchimwe ndakakumbira kuna Jehovha, ndicho chandichatsvaka: Kugara kwangu mumba maJehovha mazuva ose eupenyu hwangu, kuona kunaka kwaJehovha, nekurangarira mutembere yake.
\v	5	Nokutinezuva renjodzi anondiviga mudumba rake; achandivanza pakavanda petende rake; achandikwiridza padombo.
\v	6	Zvinoikozvino musoro wangu uchasimudzirwa pamusoro pevavengi vangu vanondikomba; naizvozvo ndichabaira zvibairo zvemufaro mutende rake. Ndichaimba, uye ndichaimba rumbidzo kuna Jehovha.
\v	7	InzwaiJehovha, inzwi rangu, ndichidana; ivaiwo netsitsi neni mugondipindura.
\v	8	Makati: Tsvakai chiso changu. Moyo wangu wakati kwamuri: Chiso chenyu, Jehovha, ndichachitsvaka.
\v	9	Regaikundivanzira chiso chenyu; musadzinga muranda wenyu pakutsamwa; maiva rubatsiro rwangu; regai kundirasa, kana kundisiya, Mwari weruponeso rwangu.
\v	10	Baba vangu namai vangu pavanondisiya, ipapo Jehovha achandiunganidza.
\v	11	Ndidzidzisei nzira yenyu Jehovha; uye munditungamirire panzira yakati chechetere, nekuda kwevavengi vangu.
\v	12	Regai kundikumikidza kuchido chevavengi vangu, nokuti zvapupu zvenhema zvandimukira, naiye anofemereka hasha.
\v	13	 Ndingadai ndakaparara kunze kwekuti ndakatenda kuti ndichaona kunaka kwaJehovha panyika yevapenyu.
\p
\v	14	Rindira Jehovha; iva nesimba, nemoyo wako usimbe; hongu, rindira Jehovha.
\c	28
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira rubatsiro
\p
\v	1	Ndichadanakwamuri, Jehovha; dombo rangu, regai kundinyararira; zvimwe  kana mukandinyararira ndingafanana nevanoburukira kugomba.
\v	2	Inzwaiinzwi remikumbiro yangu, kana ndichichemera rubatsiro kwamuri, kana ndichisimudzira maoko angu kunzvimbo yenyu yeinzwi dzvene.
\v	3	Musandikwevapamwe nevakaipa uye pamwe nevaiti vezvakaipa, ivo vanotaura rugare kuvavakidzani vavo, asi chakaipa chiri mumoyo mavo.
\v	4	Muvapezvinoenderana nezviito zvavo uye zvinoenderana neuipi hwezviito zvavo; vapei zvinotevera basa remaoko avo; dzoserai kwavari chiito chavo.
\v	5	Nokutihavana hanya nemabasa aJehovha, kana nekuita kwemaoko ake, achavaputsa nekusavavaka.
\p
\v	6	NgaarumbidzweJehovha, nokuti wakanzwa inzwi remikumbiro yangu.
\v	7	Jehovhaisimba rangu nenhovo yangu; moyo wangu wakavimba naye, uye ndakabatsirwa; naizvozvo moyo wangu wakapembera, uye ndinomurumbidza nerwiyo rwangu.
\v	8	Jehovhaisimba ravo, uye inhare yeruponeso rukuru rwemuzodzwa wake.
\v	9	Ponesaivanhu venyu, uye ropafadzai nhaka yenyu, muvafudzewo, muvatakure kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\c	29
\s	Inzwi raJehovha
\p
\v	1	Ipaikuna Jehovha, imwi vanakomana vemasimba, ipai kuna Jehovha kudzo nesimba.
\v	2	Ipaikuna Jehovha kudzo yezita rake; shumirai Jehovha mukunaka kweutsvene.
\p
\v	3	InzwiraJehovha riri pamusoro pedzimvura; Mwari wekubwinya anotinhira; Jehovha ari pamusoro pedzimvura zhinji.
\v	4	InzwiraJehovha rine simba; inzwi raJehovha rine ukuru.
\v	5	InzwiraJehovha rinovhuna misidhari; hongu, Jehovha anovhunyana misidhari yeRebhanoni.
\v	6	Anoikwakusasemhuru; Rebhanoni neSirioni semhuru yenyati.
\v	7	InzwiraJehovha rinopamura mirazvo yemoto.
\v	8	InzwiraJehovha rinozunungusa renje; Jehovha anozunungusa renje reKadheshi.
\v	9	InzwiraJehovha rinoberekesa nondo, rinosvuura masango; nemutembere yake zvose zvinoti: Rukudzo.
\p
\v	10	Jehovha agere pamusoro pemafashame; hongu, Jehovha agere ari mambo kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	11	Jehovha achapa simba kuvanhu vake; Jehovha acharopafadza vanhu vake nerugare.
\c	3
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira rubatsiro
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,vakawanda sei vadzivisi vangu! Vazhinji vanondimukira.
\v	2	Vazhinjivanoti pamusoro pemweya weupenyu wangu: Hakuna ruponeso kwaari kubva kuna Mwari. Sera.
\v	3	Asiimwi Jehovha muri nhovo kwandiri, kudzo yangu, nemusimudzi wemusoro wangu.
\v	4	Ndakadanakuna Jehovha neinzwi rangu; iye ndokundinzwa ari pagomo rake dzvene. Sera.
\v	5	Inindakarara pasi ndokubatwa nehope; ndakamuka; nokuti Jehovha anonditsigira.
\v	6	Handingatyizvuru gumi zvevanhu vakazvimisa vakandikomberedza kundirwisa.
\v	7	SimukaiJehovha, ndiponesei, Mwari wangu. Nokuti makarova vavengi vangu vose pashaya; makavhuna mazino evakaipa.
\v	8	RuponesonderwaJehovha; ropafadzo yako iri pamusoro pevanhu vako. Sera.
\c	30
\s	Rwiyo rwekuvonga
\p
\v	1	Ndichakukudzai,Jehovha, nokuti makandisimudza, uye hamuna kuita vavengi vangu vafare pamusoro pangu.
\v	2	Jehovha,Mwari wangu, ndakachema kwamuri, uye mukandirapa.
\v	3	Jehovha,makakwidza mweya weupenyu wangu kubva paSheori; makandichengeta ndiri mupenyu kuti ndirege kuburukira kugomba.
\p
\v	4	ImbiraiJehovha nziyo dzekurumbidza, imwi vatsvene vake, muvonge pachirangariro cheutsvene hwake.
\v	5	Nokuti pane chinguvana pakutsamwa kwake; asi tsitsi dzake ndedzeupenyu hwose. Pamadekwani kuchema kunopedza usiku hwose, asi pamangwanani pane mufaro.
\p
\v	6	Inindakati pakubudirira kwangu: Handingatongozununguswi.
\v	7	Jehovha,netsitsi dzenyu makamisa gomo rangu nesimba; makavanza chiso chenyu; ini ndikatambudzika.
\v	8	Ndakachemakwamuri, Jehovha; uye ndakakumbira kuna Ishe.
\v	9	Munerubatsiro rwei muropa rangu, pakuburukira kwangu kugomba? Guruva ringakurumbidzai here? Ringadudzira chokwadi chenyu here?
\v	10	Inzwai Jehovha, mundinzwirei tsitsi; Jehovha, ivai mubatsiri wangu.
\p
\v	11	Makashandura kuchema kwangu kukava kutamba; makasunungura saga rangu, mukasunga chiuno changu nemufaro;
\v	12	kuti rukudzo  rwangu rwukuimbirei nziyo dzekurumbidza, rwurege kunyarara. Jehovha Mwari wangu, ndichakuvongai nekusingaperi.
\c	31
\s	Dhavhidhi anokumbira kubatsirwa, achivonga unyoro hwaJehovha
\p
\v	1	KwamuriJehovha, ndinovimba; ndirege kutongonyadziswa; ndinunurei mukururama kwenyu.
\v	2	Rerekerainzeve yenyu kwandiri; kurumidzai kundinunura; ivai dombo rangu rakasimba, imba yenhare yakasimba yekundiponesa.
\v	3	Nokutiimwi muri dombo rangu nenhare yangu; naizvozvo nditungamirirei mundisesedze nekuda kwezita renyu.
\v	4	Ndibudiseipamumbure wavakandivanzira; nokuti imwi muri nhare yangu.
\v	5	Ndinoisamweya wangu muruoko rwenyu; makandidzikinura, Jehovha, Mwari wechokwadi.
\v	6	Ndakavengavanotarisa zvisina maturo zvenhema; asi ini ndinovimba naJehovha.
\v	7	Ndichafaranekufarisisa mutsitsi dzenyu; nokuti makaona dambudziko rangu; makaziva mweya weupenyu wangu mukumanikidzika kukuru.
\v	8	Uyehamuna kundivharira muruoko rwemuvengi; makamisa tsoka dzangu panzvimbo yakafarikana.
\p
\v	9	Ndinzwireitsitsi Jehovha, nokuti ndiri padambudziko; ziso rangu rapedzwa nekurwadziwa, mweya weupenyu wangu nemuviri wangu.
\v	10	Nokuti upenyu hwangu hwunopera nemarwadzo, nemakore angu nekugomera; simba rangu rinodzadzarika nekuda kwekutadza kwangu, uye mapfupa angu anopedzwa.
\v	11	Ndava chizvidziwa pakati pevavengi vangu vose, asi zvikuru kuvavakidzani vangu, nechityiso kuvazivikani vangu; vanondiona kunze vanonditiza.
\v	12	Ndakanganikwa sewakafa kubva pamoyo; ndava semudziyo unoparara.
\v	13	Nokuti ndakanzwa kupomera kwevazhinji, kutya kurutivi rwose, pakundirangana pamwe chete kwavo; vanoronga kutora mweya wangu.
\p
\v	14	Asi ini ndakavimba nemwi, Jehovha; ndakati: Muri Mwari wangu.
\v	15	Nguva dzangu dziri muruoko rwenyu; ndinunurei paruoko rwevavengi vangu, nepavadzingiriri vangu.
\v	16	Vhenekeresai chiso chenyu pamuranda wenyu; ndiponesei nengoni dzenyu.
\v	17	Jehovha, ngandirege kunyadziswa; nokuti ndakadana kwamuri; vakaipa ngavanyadziswe; ngavanyarare paguva.
\v	18	Miromo yenhema ngainyaradzwe, inotaura zvakaoma kurwisa wakarurama nekuzvikudza nekuzvidza.
\p
\v	19	Haiwa, kwakakura sei kururama kwenyu, kwamakaisira avo vanokutyai, makavaitira avo vanovimba nemwi pamberi pevanakomana vevanhu.
\v	20	Muchavavanza pakavanda pekuvapo kwenyu kuti vabve pamarangano emunhu; muvavige padumba pakukakavadzana kwendimi.
\v	21	Jehovha ngaavongwe, nokuti wakandiitira tsitsi dzinoshamisa paguta riri nhare.
\v	22	Nokuti ini ndakati pakukurumidza kwangu: Ndagurwa ndabviswa pamberi pemeso enyu. Zvakadaro makanzwa inzwi remikumbiro yangu pakuchema kwangu kwamuri.
\p
\v	23	Idai Jehovha, imwi mose vatsvene vake; Jehovha anochengeta vakatendeka, uye anotsiva zvikuru anoita nekuzvikudza.
\v	24	Simbai, achasimbisa moyo wenyu, imwi mose munovimba naJehovha.
\c	32
\s	Mufaro wemunhu wakakanganwirwa zvivi zvake
\p
\v	1	Wakaropafadzwauyo chitadzo chake chakakanganwirwa, chivi chake chakafukidzirwa.
\v	2	Wakaropafadzwamunhu Jehovha waasingaverengeri chakaipa, uye pasina kunyengera pamweya wake.
\p
\v	3	Pandakanyarara,mapfupa angu akakwegura nekuvovora kwangu zuva rose.
\v	4	Nokutimasikati neusiku ruoko rwenyu rwairema pamusoro pangu; unyoro hwangu hwakashandurwa hukava kuoma kwechirimo. Sera.
\p
\v	5	Ndakakuzivisaichivi changu, uye kuipa kwangu handina kuvanza; ndakati: Ndichareurura maererano nezvitadzo zvangu kuna Jehovha; uye imwi makakanganwira kuipa kwechivi changu. Sera.
\p
\v	6	Nekudakweizvi umwe neumwe anotya Mwari ngaanyengetere kwamuri panguva ya munowanikwa; zvirokwazvo pafashame redzimvura zhinji hadzisvikiri kwaari.
\v	7	Imwimuri nzvimbo yangu yekuvanda; muchandichengeta pakutambudzika; muchandikomberedza nenziyo dzekununura. Sera.
\p
\v	8	Ndichakurairanekukudzidzisa munzira yauchafamba nayo; ndichapa zano; ziso rangu riri pamusoro pako.
\v	9	Regaikuva sebhiza, senyurusi zvisina kunzwisisa; muromo waro kubatwa nemakashu nematomu, zvimwe riswedere kwauri.
\p
\v	10	Matambudziko ewakaipa akawanda; asi anovimba naJehovha, tsitsi dzichamukomba.
\v	11	Farai muna Jehovha, mupembere, imwi vakarurama; pururudzai, imwi mose vakarurama pamoyo.
\c	33
\s	Rwiyo rwekurumbidza Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Pururudzaimuna Jehovha, imwi vakarurama; kurumbidza kwakafanira vari muchokwadi.
\v	2	RumbidzaiJehovha nerudimbwa; muimbirei nemutengeranwa une hungiso gumi.
\v	3	Muimbireirwiyo rutsva; ridzai zvakanaka neruzha.
\v	4	Nokutishoko raJehovha rakarurama; nebasa rake rose riri mukutendeka.
\v	5	Anodakururama nekururamisa; nyika izere neunyoro hwaJehovha.
\p
\v	6	NeshokoraJehovha matenga akaitwa, uye hondo dzose dzawo nekufema kwemuromo wake.
\v	7	Anounganidzamvura dzegungwa semurwi; anoisa makungwa mumatura.
\v	8	Nyikayose ngaitye Jehovha; vagari vose venyika ngavadedere naye.
\v	9	Nokutiiye wakataura, zvikavapo; iye wakaraira, izvo ndokumira.
\p
\v	10	Jehovha anoparadza zano revahedheni; anoshaisa zvirongwa zvevanhu maturo.
\v	11	Zano raJehovha rinomira kusvika rinhi narinhi, mifungo yemoyo wake kuzera nezera.
\v	12	Rwakaropafadzwa rudzi Jehovha ari Mwari warwo, vanhu vaakasarudza kuva nhaka yake.
\v	13	Jehovha wakatarisa ari kumatenga; anoona vanakomana vose vevanhu.
\v	14	Ari panzvimbo yeugaro hwake anotarisa pavagari vose vepanyika.
\v	15	Iye anoumba moyo yavo vose; iye anocherekedza mabasa avo ose.
\p
\v	16	Hapana mambo anoponeswa neuwandu hwehondo; mhare hainunurwi neuwandu hwesimba.
\v	17	Bhiza harina maturo pakukunda; uye harinunuri neukuru hwesimba raro.
\v	18	Tarirai, ziso raJehovha riri pamusoro pevanomutya, pane vanorindira tsitsi dzake;
\v	19	kununura mweya weupenyu wavo parufu, nekuvararamisa panzara.
\v	20	Mweya weupenyu wedu wakarindira Jehovha; ndiye mubatsiri wedu nenhovo yedu.
\v	21	Nokuti moyo wedu uchafara maari, nokuti takavimba nezita rake dzvene.
\p
\v	22	Tsitsi dzenyu ngadzive pamusoro pedu, Jehovha, sezvatakakurindirai.
\c	34
\s	Jehovha anobatsira vanotenda kwaari
\p
\v	1	NdicharumbidzaJehovha panguva dzose; rumbidzo yake icharamba iri mumuromo mangu.
\v	2	Mweyaweupenyu wangu uchazvirumbidza muna Jehovha; vanyoro vachazvinzwa, vakafara.
\v	3	KudzaiJehovha pamwe neni; ngatisimudzire zita rake pamwe chete.
\p
\v	4	NdakatsvakaJehovha; uye akandipindura, akandinunura pakutya kwangu kose.
\v	5	Vakatarirakwaari, vakapenyeswa nemufaro; uye zviso zvavo hazvinganyadziswi.
\v	6	Murombouyu wakachema; uye Jehovha wakanzwa, akamuponesa panjodzi dzake dzose.
\v	7	MutumwawaJehovha anodzika musasa kukomberedza avo vanomutya, nekuvanunura.
\v	8	Ravirai,muone kuti Jehovha wakanaka; wakaropafadzwa murume anovimba naye.
\v	9	ItyaiJehovha, imwi vatsvene vake; nokuti vanomutya havana chinoshaikwa.
\v	10	Vana veshumba vanoshaiwa, vane nzara; asi avo vanotsvaka Jehovha havashaiwi chipi nechipi chakanaka.
\p
\v	11	Uyai imwi vana, munditeerere; ndichakudzidzisai kutya Jehovha.
\v	12	Ndoupi munhu anoshuva upenyu, anoda mazuva kuti aone zvakanaka?
\v	13	Chengeta rurimi rwako kubva pane zvakaipa, nemiromo yako irege kutaura zvinonyengera.
\v	14	Ibva pazvakaipa, uite zvakanaka; tsvaka rugare, umhanye kurutevera.
\v	15	Meso aJehovha ari pavakarurama, uye nzeve dzake dziri pakuchema kwavo.
\v	16	Chiso chaJehovha chinorwisa vanoita zvakaipa, kuti agure chiyeuchidzo chavo panyika.
\v	17	Vakadana, uye Jehovha wakanzwa, akavanunura panjodzi dzavo dzose.
\v	18	Jehovha ari pedo nevane moyo yakaputsika, anoponesa vane mweya yakapwanyika.
\v	19	Matambudziko ewakarurama mazhinji; asi Jehovha anomununura kubva paari ose.
\v	20	Anochengeta mapfupa ake ose; hakuna nerimwe rawo rinovhuniwa.
\v	21	Zvakaipa zvichauraya wakaipa; uye vanovenga wakarurama vachapiwa mhosva.
\v	22	Jehovha anodzikinura mweya weupenyu wevaranda vake; uye vose vanovimba naye havangapiwi mhosva.
\c	35
\s	Dhavhidhi anokumbira kuti vakaipa varohwe
\p
\v	1	Kakavadzanai,Jehovha, nevanokakavadzana neni; irwai nevanorwa neni.
\v	2	Batisisainhovo huru nenhovo diki, musimukire rubatsiro rwangu.
\v	3	Vhomoraiwopfumo, mudzivire  nzira kurwisa vadzingiriri vangu; itii kumweya weupenyu wangu: Ndiri ruponeso rwako.
\p
\v	4	Ngavanyadziswevazvidzwe vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu; ngavadzoserwe shure vavhiringidzwe vanorongera dambudziko rangu.
\v	5	Ngavavesehundi pamberi pemhepo; uye mutumwa waJehovha ngaa vasunde.
\v	6	Nzirayavo ngaive rima, itedze kwazvo; uye mutumwa waJehovha avadzingirire.
\v	7	Nokutipasina chikonzero vakandivanzira mumbure wavo  mugomba; pasina chikonzero vakacherera mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	8	Kuparadzwangakusvike kwaari akarivara; uye mumbure wake waakavanza ngaumubate iye; ngaawire mauri pakuparadzwa.
\p
\v	9	Asimweya weupenyu wangu uchafarira Jehovha; uchapembera muruponeso rwake.
\v	10	Mapfupa angu ose achati: Jehovha, ndiani wakaita semwi, munonunura murombo pane ane simba kumupfuura, hongu murombo nemushaiwi pane anomupamba?
\p
\v	11	Zvapupu zvezvakaipa zvinosimuka; vanondibvunza zvandisingazivi.
\v	12	Vanonditsivira zvakaipa pachinzvimbo chezvakanaka; mune mariro mumweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	13	Asi kana ndiri ini, pakurwara kwavo chipfeko changu chaiva saga; ndakaninipisa mweya weupenyu wangu nekutsanya, uye munyengetero wangu wakadzokera muchipfuva changu.
\v	14	Ndakafamba sezvinonzi ishamwari uye sezvinonzi ihama kwandiri; ndakakotama kuchema seanochema mai.
\v	15	Asi pakugumburwa kwangu vakafara, vakaungana pamwe; vakarasiwa vakaungana kundirwisa, zvino ndaiva ndisingazivi; vakabvambura vakasamira.
\v	16	Sevakaipa vanodadira pamabiko vakandigedera mazino avo.
\p
\v	17	Ishe, muchatarisa kusvika rinhi? Dzosai mweya weupenyu wangu pakuparadza kwavo, mudikanwi wangu padzishumba.
\v	18	Ndichakuvongai paungano huru; ndichakurumbidzai pakati pevanhu vane simba.
\p
\v	19	Varege kufara pamusoro pangu avo vari vavengi vangu zvenhema,  kana ngavabwaire ziso ivo vanondivenga pasina chikonzero.
\v	20	Nokuti havatauri rugare; asi vanoronga mashoko eunyengeri kurwisa vakanyarara panyika.
\v	21	Zvino vakandishamisira muromo wavo zvikuru, vakati: Hekani, hekani! Meso edu akazviona.
\v	22	Maka zviona, Jehovha; regai kunyarara; Ishe, regai kuva kure neni.
\v	23	Zvimutsei, mumukire mutongo wangu, nyaya yangu, Mwari wangu naIshe wangu.
\v	24	Nditongerei, Jehovha Mwari wangu, zvichienderana nekururama kwenyu, uye ngavarege kufara pamusoro pangu.
\v	25	Ngavarege kuti mumoyo wavo: Hekani, chishuvo chedu; ngavarege kuti: Tamumedza.
\v	26	Ngavanyadziswe, vazvidzwe pamwe chete, vanofarira padambudziko rangu; ngavafukidzwe nekunyara nekuzvidzwa, ivo vanozvikudza pamusoro pangu.
\p
\v	27	Ngavadanidzire nemufaro, vafare, ivo vanoshuva kururama kwangu; hongu ngavati rinhi narinhi: Ngaakudzwe Jehovha, iye anoshuva rugare rwemuranda wake.
\v	28	Zvino rurimi rwangu rwuchataura kururama kwenyu, zuva rose kurumbidzwa kwenyu.
\c	36
\s	Kuipa kwewakaipa nekunaka kwaMwari
\p
\v	1	Nhaurwayekupanduka kune wakaipa  iri mumoyo mangu: Hakuna kutya Mwari pamberi pemeso ake.
\v	2	Nokutianozvinyengera pameso ake, uipi hwake kusvika hwawanikwa huchivengeka.
\v	3	Mashokoemuromo wake uipi neunyengeri; anoguma kuchenjera  nekuita zvakanaka.
\v	4	Anorongachakaipa pamubhedha wake; anozvimisa panzira isina kunaka; haarambi chakaipa.
\p
\v	5	Jehovha,ngoni dzenyu dziri kumatenga; kutendeka kwenyu kunosvika kumakore.
\v	6	Kururamakwenyu kwakaita semakomo makuru; mitongo yenyu udziku ukuru; Jehovha, munoponesa munhu nemhuka.
\v	7	Rwakakoshasei rudo rweunyoro hwenyu, Mwari! Naizvozvo vana vevanhu vanotsvaka utiziro pamumvuri wemapapiro enyu.
\v	8	Vachagutswakwazvo nezvakakora zveimba yenyu; uye muchavanwisa  parwizi rwemafaro enyu.
\v	9	Nokutikwamuri kune chitubu cheupenyu; muchiedza chenyu tichaona chiedza.
\v	10	Ruenderere mberi rudo rweunyoro hwenyu kune vanokuzivai, nekururama kwenyu kune vakarurama pamoyo.
\p
\v	11	Rutsoka rwevanozvikudza ngarurege kusvika kwandiri; neruoko rwewakaipa ngarurege kundidzungaidza.
\v	12	Ndipo vabati vezvakaipa pavawira; vawisirwa pasi uye havagoni kumuka.
\c	37
\s	Mufaro wevakaipa ndewenguva diki
\p
\v	1	Usashungurudzikanekuda kwevaiti vezvakaipa; usagodora vabati vezvakaipa.
\v	2	Nokutivachakurumidza kugurwa seuswa, nekusvava seuswa unyoro.
\v	3	VimbanaJehovha, uye ita zvakanaka; gara panyika, uye uzvifunde  nekutendeka.
\v	4	Uyezvifadze muna Jehovha; zvino achapa kwauri mikumbiro yemoyo wako.
\v	5	Ipanzira yako kuna Jehovha; vimbawo naye; zvino iye achazviita.
\v	6	Uyeachabudisa kururama kwako sechiedza, nemutongo wako semasikati makuru.
\v	7	Nyararapana Jehovha, umurindire; usazvishungurudza pamusoro peanobudirira nenzira yake, pamusoro pemunhu anoita mazano akaipa.
\v	8	Regakutsamwa, usiye hasha; usazvishungurudza, zvinongo pinza chete mukuita zvakaipa.
\v	9	Nokutivaiti vezvakaipa vachagurwa; asi vanorindira Jehovha, ivo vachagara nhaka yenyika.
\v	10	Pachine chi nguvana, wakaipa haachazovipo; kunyange ukacherekedza nzvimbo yake, achange asipo.
\v	11	Asi vanyoro vachagara nhaka yenyika; uye vachazvifadza neuwandu hwerugare.
\v	12	Wakaipa anorongera wakarurama, nekumugedera mazino ake.
\v	13	Ishe achamuseka; nokuti anoona kuti zuva rake rinouya.
\v	14	Vakaipa vakavhomora munondo, uye vakawembura uta hwavo, kuwisira pasi murombo neanoshaiwa, kuuraya wakarurama panzira.
\v	15	Munondo wavo uchapinda pamoyo yavo, uye uta hwavo uzhinji huchavhuniwa.
\v	16	Chishoma wakarurama chaanacho chiri nani pane pfuma yevakaipa vazhinji.
\v	17	Nokuti maoko evakaipa achavhuniwa; asi Jehovha anotsigira vakarurama.
\v	18	Jehovha anoziva mazuva evakarurama; uye nhaka yavo ichava nekusingaperi.
\v	19	Havanganyadziswi nenguva yekuipa; nepamazuva enzara vachaguta.
\v	20	Asi vakaipa vachaparara; uye vavengi vaJehovha vachanyangarika sekubwinya kwemafuro; vachanyangarika muutsi.
\v	21	Wakaipa anokwereta asingadzoreri; asi wakarurama ane tsitsi, anopa.
\v	22	Nokuti vakaropafadzwa naye vachagara nhaka yenyika; asi vakatukwa naye vachagurwa.
\v	23	Nhanho dzemunhu  wakarurama dzinoruramiswa naJehovha; uye anofarira munzira yake.
\v	24	Kunyange akawa, haangarasirwi pasi; nokuti Jehovha anotsigira ruoko rwake.
\v	25	Ndaiva mudiki, zvino ndakwegura; zvakadaro handina kuona wakarurama achisiiwa, nembeu yake ichitsvaka zvekudya.
\v	26	Zuva rose ane tsitsi, uye anopa chikwereti; nembeu yake iropafadzo.
\v	27	Ibva pane zvakaipa, uye ita zvakanaka; ugare kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	28	Nokuti Jehovha anoda mutongo; uye haangasii vatsvene vake; vachachengetedzwa kusvika rinhi narinhi; asi mbeu yevakaipa ichagurwa.
\v	29	Vakarurama vachagara nhaka yenyika, uye vachagaramo kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	30	Muromo wewakarurama unoreva uchenjeri; nerurimi rwake rwunotaura mutongo.
\v	31	Murau waMwari wake uri mumoyo make; nhanho dzake hadzitedzemuki.
\v	32	Wakaipa anochenjerera wakarurama, uye anotsvaka kumuuraya.
\v	33	Jehovha haangamusii muruoko rwake; uye haangamupi mhosva paanotongwa.
\v	34	Rindira Jehovha, uye chengeta nzira yake; zvino achakukudza kuti ugare nhaka yenyika; panogurwa vakaipa uchaona.
\v	35	Ndakaona wakaipa anotyisa, achitandavara semuti munyoro panyika yawo yechisikigo.
\v	36	Zvakadaro anopfuura, zvino tarira, haa chipo, hongu, ndakamutsvaka asi haana kuwanikwa.
\v	37	Cherekedzai wakaperera, muone wakarurama; nokuti kuguma kwemunhu  uyu rugare.
\v	38	Asi vadariki vachaparadzwa pamwe chete; kuguma kwevakaipa kuchagurwa.
\v	39	Asi ruponeso rwevakarurama rwunobva kuna Jehovha, nhare yavo panguva yekutambudzika.
\v	40	Zvino Jehovha anovabatsira, nekuvanunura; achavanunura kune vakaipa, nekuvaponesa, nokuti vanotizira kwaari.
\c	38
\s	Munyengetero wemunhu anotambudzika
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,regai kunditsiura pakutsamwa kwenyu, kana kundiranga pakupfuta kwehasha dzenyu.
\v	2	Nokutimiseve yenyu yakanyura mandiri, uye ruoko rwenyu rwunonyura pamusoro pangu.
\v	3	Hapanautano munyama yangu nekuda kwekutsamwa kwenyu; hakuna rugare mumapfupa angu nekuda kwechivi changu.
\v	4	Nokutizvitadzo zvangu zvapfuura musoro wangu; semutoro unorema zvinondiremera kwazvo.
\v	5	Marondaangu anonhuhwa akaora nekuda kweupenzi hwangu.
\v	6	Ndakakombamiswa,ndakakotamiswa kupfuurikidza; zuva rose ndinofamba ndichichema.
\v	7	Nokutichiuno changu chizere neutsva; uye hapana utano panyama yangu.
\v	8	Ndakarukutika,ndakakuika zvikuru kwazvo; ndakavovora nekuda kwekugomera kwemoyo wangu.
\p
\v	9	Ishe,chishuvo changu chose chiri pamberi penyu, uye kugomera kwangu hakuna kuvanziwa kwamuri.
\v	10	Moyo wangu unorova; simba rangu randisiya; uye chiedza chemeso angu, naicho hachipo pandiri.
\v	11	Vanondida neshamwari dzangu vanomira kure nehosha yangu; nevavakidzani vangu vanomira kure.
\v	12	Avowo vanotsvaka upenyu hwangu vanoisa misungo; uye vanotsvaka kukuvara kwangu vanotaura kuparadza kukuru, nekufunga unyengeri ukuru zuva rose.
\p
\v	13	Asi ini ndakaita sematsi, handinzwi, uye sembeveve isingashamisi muromo wayo.
\v	14	Hongu ndakaita semunhu asinganzwi, uye pasina makakava pamuromo wake.
\v	15	Nokuti kwamuri, Jehovha, ndinovimba; imwi muchapindura, Ishe Mwari wangu.
\v	16	Nokuti ndakati: Zvimwe vafare pamusoro pangu. Panotedzemuka rutsoka rwangu vanozvikudza kupikisana neni.
\v	17	Nokuti ndava pedo nekukamhina; nemarwadzo angu ari pamberi pangu rinhi narinhi.
\v	18	Nokuti ndichazivisa uipi hwangu; ndichashungurudzika nechivi changu.
\v	19	Asi vavengi vangu vapenyu vane simba; nevanondivenga pasina chikonzero vawanda.
\v	20	Naivowo vanotsiva chakaipa pachinzvimbo chechakanaka vavengi vangu, nokuti ndinoteverera chakanaka.
\p
\v	21	Regai kundisiya, Jehovha; Mwari wangu, musava kure neni.
\v	22	Kurumidzai kundibatsira, Ishe, ruponeso rwangu.
\c	39
\s	Munyengetero pakutambudzika
\p
\v	1	Ndakati:Ndichachenjerera nzira dzangu, kuti ndirege kutadza nerurimi rwangu; ndichachengeta muromo wangu netomu, kana wakaipa achipo pamberi pangu.
\v	2	Ndaivambeveve  nekunyarara, ndakanyararira zvakanaka; uye kutambudzika kwangu kwakamutswa.
\v	3	Moyowangu waipisa mukati mangu; mukurangarira kwangu moto wakapfuta; ndakataura nerurimi rwangu:
\v	4	Jehovha,ndizivisei mugumo wangu, uye chiyero chemazuva angu kuti chakadii; kuti ndizive kuti ndinopfuura zvakadii.
\v	5	Tarirai,makaita mazuva angu ave upamhi hwechanza; nezera rangu sechinhu pasina pamberi penyu; zvirokwazvo, munhu umwe neumwe pakumira kwake haana maturo zvachose. Sera.
\v	6	Zvirokwazvo,munhu umwe neumwe anofamba-famba semumvuri; zvirokwazvo, vanoshungurudzika pasina; anounganidza, asi haazivi kuti ndiani achazvivuta.
\p
\v	7	Uyezvino, Ishe, ndakarindirei? Tariro yangu iri mamuri.
\v	8	Ndinunureipakudarika kwangu kose; regai kundiita chiseko chebenzi.
\v	9	Ndaivandiri mbeveve, handina kushamisa muromo wangu; nokuti ndimwi makaita.
\v	10	Bvisai shamhu yenyu kwandiri; ini ndapedzwa nehasha dzeruoko rwenyu.
\v	11	 Pamunoraira munhu nekutsiura nekuda kwechitadzo, munoita kunaka kwake kunyunguduke sechipfukuto; zvirokwazvo munhu umwe neumwe haasi chinhu. Sera.
\p
\v	12	Inzwai munyengetero wangu, Jehovha; uye ipai nzeve kukuchema kwangu; regai kunyarara pamisodzi yangu; nokuti ndiri mweni kwamuri, mutorwa, semadzibaba angu ose.
\v	13	Regai kunditarisa, kuti ndibukire, ndisati ndabva, uye ndive ndisi sipo.
\c	4
\s	Mufaro nerugare zviri kuna Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Ndipindureipakudana kwangu, Mwari wekururama kwangu; pakumanikidzwa makapa  nzvimbo yakafaranuka kwandiri. Ivai nengoni kwandiri, mugonzwa munyengetero wangu.
\v	2	Imwivanakomana vevanhu, kusvika rinhi  muchishandura rukudzo rwangu kuva chinyadzo, muchida zvisina maturo, muchitsvaka nhema? Sera.
\v	3	Asizivai kuti Jehovha wakazvitsaurira anotya Mwari; Jehovha anondinzwa pandinodana kwaari.
\v	4	Dederai,murege kutadza; tauriranai nemoyo wenyu pamubhedha wenyu, uye muve vakanyarara. Sera.
\v	5	Ipaizvibairo zvekururama, muvimbe naJehovha.
\v	6	Vazhinjivanoti: Ndiani achatiratidza zvakanaka? Jehovha simudzirai pamusoro pedu chiedza chechiso chenyu.
\v	7	Makaisamufaro mumoyo mangu kupfuura nguva iyo zviyo zvavo newaini itsva yavo zvawanzwa.
\v	8	Ndichazvambararanerugare, ndibve ndabatwa nehope; nokuti imwi moga Jehovha munondigarisa mukuchengetedzeka.
\c	40
\s	Mufaro wemunhu anotenda kuna Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Ndakarindira-rindiraJehovha; uye wakarerekera kwandiri, ndokunzwa kuchema kwangu.
\v	2	Akandinyururawopagomba rekuparadzwa, mudziva rematope, ndokuisa tsoka dzangu padombo, akasimbisa nhanho dzangu.
\v	3	Zvinowakaisa rwiyo rutsva mumuromo mangu, rumbidzo kuna Mwari wedu; vazhinji vachazviona ndokutya, uye vachavimba naJehovha.
\v	4	Wakaropafadzwamunhu anoita Jehovha chivimbo chake, uye asingacheukiri kune vanozvikudza, neavo vanotsaukira kunhema.
\v	5	Imwimakaita zvishamiso zvenyu zvive zvizhinji, Jehovha Mwari wangu, nemifungo yenyu kwatiri; hapana angaenzaniswa nemwi. Ndikada kuzvirondedzera nekuzvireva, zvakawandisa kuti zviverengwe.
\v	6	Chibaironechipo hamushuvi; makazarura nzeve dzangu; chipo chinopiswa nechipo chezvivi hamuna kuzvireva.
\v	7	Ipapondakati: Tarirai ndauya; murugwaro rwakapetwa makanyorwa nezvangu.
\v	8	Ndinofarirakuita chido chenyu, Mwari wangu; hongu, murau wenyu uri mukati meura hwangu.
\v	9	Ndakaparidzakururama paungano huru; tarira, handina kudzora miromo yangu, Jehovha, imwi munoziva.
\v	10	Handina kuvanza kururama kwenyu pakati pemoyo wangu; ndakataura kutendeka kwenyu neruponeso rwenyu; handina kuvanza rudo rweunyoro hwenyu nechokwadi chenyu kuungano huru.
\p
\v	11	Imwi, Jehovha, musandinyima tsitsi dzenyu; rudo rweunyoro hwenyu nechokwadi chenyu ngazvindichengete rinhi narinhi.
\v	12	Nokuti zvakaipa zvisingaverengeki zvakandikomba; zvitadzo zvangu zvakandibata zvekuti handigoni kuona; zvakawanda kupfuura bvudzi remusoro wangu; naizvozvo moyo wangu wandisiya.
\v	13	Zvikufadzei, Jehovha kundinunura; Jehovha kurumidzai kurubatsiro rwangu.
\v	14	Ngavanyadziswe vazvidzwe pamwe chete avo vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu kuuparadza; ngavadzoserwe shure vashorwe ivo vanoshuva chakaipa changu.
\v	15	Ngavaparadzwe uve mubairo wenyadzi dzavo vanoti kwandiri: Hekani waro, hekani waro!
\v	16	Vose vanokutsvakai ngavafare vapembere mamuri; vanoda ruponeso rwenyu ngavati rinhi narinhi: Ngaakudzwe Jehovha!
\v	17	Asi ndiri murombo nemushaiwi; Ishe anondirangarira; ndimwi mubatsiri wangu nemununuri wangu; Mwari wangu, musanonoka.
\c	41
\s	Munyengetero pakurwara
\p
\v	1	Wakaropafadzwaanorangarira murombo; Jehovha achamununura nezuva rechakaipa.
\v	2	Jehovhaachamuchengetedza, nekumuraramisa; achava wakaropafadzwa panyika; uye hamungamukumikidzi kuchido chevavengi vake.
\v	3	Jehovhaachamutsigira panhovo yeurwere; muchashandura nhovo yake yose pahosha yake.
\p
\v	4	Inindakati: Jehovha, ndinzwirei tsitsi; poresai mweya weupenyu wangu; nokuti ndakakutadzirai.
\v	5	Vavengivangu vanotaura kuipa pamusoro pangu  vachiti: Achafa rinhi, zita rake rirove?
\v	6	Kunyangekana achiuya kuona, anotaura zvisina maturo; moyo wake unozviunganidzira uipi; anobuda panze, ndokutaura.
\v	7	Vosevanondivenga vanoita zeve-zeve pamwe chete kundirwisa; vanondirongera zvakaipa kwandiri;  vachiti:
\v	8	Chinhuchakaipa chakanamatira paari; uye sezvo akarara pasi, haachamukizve.
\v	9	Hongu,murume weushamwari hwangu wandaivimba maari, aidya chingwa changu, wakandisimudzira chichitsinho.
\p
\v	10	Asi imwi, Jehovha, ndinzwirei tsitsi, mugondisimudzira, kuti ndivatsive.
\v	11	Neizvi ndinoziva kuti munofadzwa neni, nokuti muvengi wangu haana kufara pamusoro pangu.
\v	12	Kana ndiri ini, munonditsigira pauchokwadi hwangu; uye munondiisa pamberi penyu kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\p
\v	13	Ngaarumbidzwe Jehovha, Mwari waIsraeri, kubva pakusingaperi kusvika pakusingaperi. Ameni, uye Ameni.
\c	42
\s	Chishuvo chemutapwa kushumira Jehovha patembere
\p
\v	1	Senondoinotakwairira hova dzemvura, saizvozvo mweya weupenyu wangu unokutakwairirai, Mwari.
\v	2	Mweyaweupenyu wangu une nyota kuna Mwari, kuna Mwari mupenyu; ndichasvika rinhi ndionekwe pamberi pechiso chaMwari?
\v	3	Misodziyangu yanga iri zvekudya zvangu masikati neusiku, pavanoti kwandiri zuva rose: Mwari wako aripi?
\v	4	Ndinorangarirazvinhu izvi, ndichidurura mweya weupenyu wangu mukati mangu, nokuti ndakaenda nechaunga, ndakaenda navo kuimba yaMwari neinzwi remufaro nerumbidzo, chaunga chaichengetedza mabiko.
\p
\v	5	Unokotamirei,mweya weupenyu wangu, uye unoshushikanire i mukati mangu? Tarira kuna Mwari; nokuti ndichazomupa kuvonga, ruponeso rukuru rwechiso chake.
\v	6	Mwariwangu, mweya weupenyu wangu wakakotama mukati mangu; naizvozvo ndichakurangarirai ndiri panyika yaJoridhani, neHerimoni, pachikomo cheMizari.
\v	7	Udzikuhunodana udziku pakutinhira kwemapopopo enyu; mafungu enyu ose nemaboporodzi enyu akapfuura nepamusoro pangu.
\v	8	Jehovhaacharaira rudo rweunyoro hwake masikati, nepausiku rwiyo rwake ruchava neni, munyengetero kuna Mwari weupenyu hwangu.
\v	9	Ndichatikuna Mwari, dombo rangu: Makandikanganwirei? Ndinofambirei ndichichema nekuda kwemanikidzo yemuvengi?
\v	10	Neguyo pamapfupa angu, vavengi vangu vanondimhura, pavanoti kwandiri zuva rose: Mwari wako aripi?
\p
\v	11	Unokotamirei, mweya weupenyu wangu? Uye unoshushikanirei mukati mangu? Tarira kuna Mwari; nokuti ndichazomupa kuvonga, ruponeso rukuru rwechiso changu, naMwari wangu.
\c	43
\s	Munyengetero wemunhu ari muutapwa
\p
\v	1	NditongeiMwari, mureverere nyaya yangu parudzi rwusingatyi Mwari; ndinunurei pamunhu weunyengeri nekusakarurama.
\v	2	Nokutiimwi muri Mwari weutiziro hwangu; mandirasirei? Ndinofambirei ndichichema nekuda kwemanikidzo yemuvengi?
\v	3	Tumaichiedza chenyu nechokwadi chenyu; ngazvinditungamirire; ngazvindisvitse kugomo renyu dzvene, nekutabhenakeri dzenyu.
\v	4	Ipapondichaenda kuaritari yaMwari, kuna Mwari, mufaro wekufara kwangu. Hongu, ndichakurumbidzai nembira, Mwari, Mwari wangu.
\p
\v	5	Unokotamirei,mweya weupenyu wangu? Uye unoshushikanirei mukati mangu? Tarira kuna Mwari; nokuti ndichazomupa kuvonga, ruponeso rukuru rwechiso changu, naMwari wangu.
\c	44
\s	Vanhu vaMwari vanochema kwaari pakutambudzika kwavo
\p
\v	1	Mwari,takanzwa nenzeve dzedu; madzibaba edu akatirondedzera; basa ramakabata pamazuva avo, pamazuva ekare.
\v	2	Imwineruoko rwenyu makadzinga vahedheni panhaka, ndokuvasima ivo; makatambudza marudzi, asi makavaparadzira.
\v	3	Nokutihavana kugara nhaka yenyika nemunondo wavo, neruoko rwavo haruna kupa ruponeso kwavari; asi chanza chenyu cherudyi, neruoko rwenyu, nechiedza chechiso chenyu, nokuti maifadzwa navo.
\p
\v	4	Ndimwimambo wangu, Mwari; rairai kusunungurwa kukuru kwaJakove.
\v	5	Nemwitichasunda vavengi vedu; nezita renyu tichatsikira pasi vanotimukira.
\v	6	Nokutihandingavimbi neuta hwangu, nemunondo wangu haungandiponesi.
\v	7	Asimakatiponesa pavavengi vedu, uye makanyadzisa vanotivenga.
\v	8	MunaMwari tinozvirumbidza zuva rose, uye ticharumbidza zita renyu kusvika rinhi narinhi. Sera.
\p
\v	9	Asimakarasa uye makatinyadzisa; uye hamuchabudi nehondo dzedu.
\v	10	Makatidzoseresa shure kubva pamuvengi wedu; uye vanotivenga vanozvitapira.
\v	11	Makatipa semakwai kuva zvekudya, uye makatiparadzira pakati pevahedheni.
\v	12	Munotengesa vanhu venyu pasina fuma, uye hamuwedzeri  chinhu nemutengo wavo.
\v	13	Munotiita chinyadzo kuvavakidzani vedu, chiseko nechizvidzwa kune vakatipoteredza.
\v	14	Munotiita dimikira pakati pevahedheni, kudzungudzwa kwemusoro pakati pevanhu.
\v	15	Zuva rose kuzvidzwa kwangu kuri pamberi pangu; nechinyadzo chechiso changu chakandifukidza;
\v	16	nekuda kweinzwi remutuki nemuzvidzi; nekuda kwemuvengi nemutsivi.
\p
\v	17	Izvi zvose zvatiwira; zvakadaro hatina kukukanganwai, uye hatina kuita nekunyengedza pasungano yenyu.
\v	18	Moyo yedu haina kudzokera shure, kana nhanho dzedu kutsauka pagwara renyu.
\v	19	Kunyange makatipwanya-pwanya panzvimbo yemabukanana, mukatifukidza nemumvuri werufu.
\v	20	Kana tichinge takanganwa zita raMwari wedu, kana kutandavadzira maoko edu kuna mwari wendudzi:
\v	21	Mwari haanganzveri izvi here? Nokuti anoziva zvakavanzika zvemoyo.
\v	22	Zvirokwazvo, nekuda kwenyu tinourawa zuva rose; tinotorwa semakwai ekubaiwa.
\v	23	Pepukai, munorarirei, Ishe? Mukai, musa tirasa nekusingaperi.
\v	24	Munovanzirei chiso chenyu, muchikanganwa matambudziko edu nemanikidzo dzedu?
\v	25	Nokuti mweya weupenyu wedu wakotamira kuguruva; dumbu redu rinonamatira pavhu.
\v	26	Simukirai rubatsiro rwedu, uye tidzikunurei nekuda kwetsitsi dzenyu.
\c	45
\s	Rwiyo pamutambo waMambo Mukuru
\p
\v	1	Moyowangu unotutuma nyaya yakanaka; ndinotaura zvinhu zvandakaitira mambo; rurimi rwangu ipeni yemunyori anokurumidza.
\p
\v	2	Imwimakanaka kupfuura vana vevanhu; nyasha yakadururirwa pamiromo yenyu; naizvozvo Mwari wakakuropafadzai nekusingaperi.
\v	3	Sungaimunondo wenyu pachidya, Wemasimba, ukuru hwenyu neumambo hwenyu.
\v	4	Nemuumambo hwenyu, tasvai mubudirire, nekuda kwechokwadi neunyoro  nekururama; neruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwukudzidzisei zvinhu zvinotyisa.
\v	5	Miseveyenyu inopinza pamoyo yevavengi vamambo; marudzi achawa pasi penyu.
\v	6	Chigarochenyu cheushe, Mwari, chiripo nekusingaperi-peri; tsvimbo yeushe hwenyu itsvimbo yekururama.
\v	7	Munodakururama, uye munovenga kuipa; naizvozvo Mwari, Mwari wenyu, wakakuzodzai nemafuta emufaro kupfuura shamwari dzenyu.
\v	8	Nguvodzenyu dzose imura nearosi  neakasia, kubva pamizinda yenyanga dzenzou, pavakakufadzai nazvo.
\v	9	Vakundavemadzimambo vari pakati pevanhukadzi venyu vanokudzwa; vahosi vamambo vamire paruoko rwerudyi rwako, vakapfeka goridhe reOfiri.
\p
\v	10	Teerera, mukunda, uye ona, uye rereka nzeve yako; kanganwawo vanhu vekwako, neimba yababa vako.
\v	11	Ipapo mambo achashuva kunaka kwako; nokuti ndiye Ishe wako; umukotamire.
\v	12	Nemukunda weTire, vafumi pakati pevanhu, vachakumbira chiso chako nechipo.
\v	13	Mukunda wamambo anobwinya kose mukati; nguvo yake ndeye mabasa akarukwa egoridhe.
\v	14	Uchaperekwa kuna mambo akapfeka nguvo dzine mavara-mavara; mhandara, shamwari dzake dzinomutevera, vachaiswa kwamuri.
\v	15	Vachaperekwa nemafaro nekufarisisa; vachapinda mumuzinda wamambo.
\v	16	Panzvimbo yemadzibaba ako pachava nevana vako; achavagadza vave machinda panyika yose.
\v	17	Ndicharangaridza zita renyu pamazera ose; naizvozvo marudzi achakurumbidzai kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\c	46
\s	Mwari utiziro hwedu
\p
\v	1	Mwariutiziro hwedu nesimba, wakaratidzwa kuva rubatsiro rukuru pamatambudziko.
\v	2	Naizvozvohatingatyi pakushanduka kwenyika, kunyange makomo akasudzunukira mukati memakungwa.
\v	3	Mvurazhinji yawo ngaitinhire imutswe, makomo adedere nekupupuma kwawo. Sera.
\v	4	Rwizi rwuripo, hova dzawo dzichafadza guta raMwari, nzvimbo tsvene yedzitabhenakeri dzeWekumusoro-soro.
\v	5	Mwariari mukati maro; haringazununguswi; Mwari acharibatsira pakuonekwa kwemangwanani.
\v	6	Vahedhenivakabvongodzeka; ushe hwakazununguka; wakabudisa inzwi rake; nyika ikanyunguduka.
\v	7	Jehovhawehondo anesu; Mwari waJakove inhare yedu. Sera.
\v	8	Uyaimuone mabasa aJehovha, uyo anoisa kuparadza kukuru panyika.
\v	9	Anogumisadzihondo kusvika pakuguma kwenyika; anovhuna uta, nekugura pfumo; anopisa dzingoro mumoto.
\p
\v	10	Nyararai, muzive kuti ndini Mwari; ndichasimudzirwa pakati pevahedheni, ndichasimudzirwa panyika.
\v	11	Jehovha wehondo anesu; Mwari waJakove inhare yedu. Sera.
\c	47
\s	Marudzi ose ngaarumbidze Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Uchirai,imwi marudzi ose! Pururudzai kuna Mwari neinzwi remufaro.
\v	2	NokutiJehovha Wekumusoro-soro anotyisa; ndiMambo mukuru pamusoro penyika yose.
\v	3	Achaisavanhu pasi pedu, nemarudzi pasi petsoka dzedu.
\v	4	Achatisarudziranhaka yedu, ruremekedzo rwaJakove waanoda. Sera.
\p
\v	5	Mwariwakwira nekudanidzira, Jehovha nekurira kwehwamanda.
\v	6	ImbiraiMwari rumbidzo, imbai rumbidzo; imbirai mambo wedu rumbidzo, imbai rumbidzo.
\v	7	NokutiMwari ndiMambo wepasi pose; imbai rumbidzo  nekunzwisisa.
\v	8	Mwarianotonga pamusoro pevahedheni; Mwari agere pachigaro cheushe cheutsvene hwake.
\v	9	Machindaevanhu aungana pamwe, vanhu vaMwari waAbhurahama. Nokuti nhovo dzepanyika ndedzaMwari; wakakwiridzirwa kwazvo.
\c	48
\s	Ziyoni guta raMambo Mukuru
\p
\v	1	MukuruJehovha, uye ndewekurumbidzwa kukuru, muguta raMwari wedu, gomo rake dzvene.
\v	2	Rakanakapakukwirira, mufaro wenyika yose igomo reZiyoni,  pamativi ekumaodzanyemba, guta raMambo mukuru.
\v	3	Pamizindayake Mwari anozikanwa kuti inhare.
\v	4	Nokutitarirai, madzimambo akaungana, akapfuura pamwe chete.
\v	5	Ivovaka riona, saka vakashamiswa, vakavhunduka, vakakurumidza kutiza.
\v	6	Kudederakwakavabatapo; kurwadziwa sekwemukadzi anopona.
\v	7	Munoputsazvikepe zveTarishishi nemhepo yemabvazuva.
\v	8	Sezvatakanzwa,saizvozvo takaona muguta raJehovha wehondo, muguta raMwari wedu; Mwari acharisimbisa nekusingaperi. Sera.
\p
\v	9	Takafungazverudo rweunyoro hwenyu, Mwari, mukati metembere yenyu.
\v	10	Sezita renyu Mwari, ndizvo zvakaita rumbidzo yenyu kusvika kumigumo yenyika; ruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwuzere nekururama.
\v	11	Gomo reZiyoni ngarifare, vakunda vaJudha ngavafarisise, nekuda kwemitongo yenyu.
\v	12	Poteredzai Ziyoni, muritenderedze; muverenge shongwe dzaro.
\v	13	Isai moyo yenyu kurusvingo rwaro, gurai muongorore mizinda yaro, kuti murondedzere zera rinotevera.
\v	14	Nokuti Mwari uyu ndiMwari wedu rinhi narinhi; iye achatitungamirira kusvika parufu.
\c	49
\s	Zvose zvepanyika zvinopfuura
\p
\v	1	Inzwaichinhu ichi, vanhu vose. Ipai nzeve, vagari vose vepanyika.
\v	2	Zvosevakaderera nevakakwirira, mufumi nemurombo pamwe chete.
\v	3	Muromowangu uchataura zvenjere; uye murangariro wemoyo wangu uchava njere zhinji.
\v	4	Ndicharerekeranzeve yangu kufananidzo; ndichadudza dimikira rangu nembira.
\p
\v	5	Ndichatyireipamazuva ezvakaipa,  kana uipi hwevari pazvitsitsinho zvangu huchindikomberedza?
\v	6	Vanovimbanefuma yavo, nekuzvikudza pakuwanda kwefuma yavo:
\v	7	Munhuhaatongodzikunuri hama  yake, haangapi Mwari rudzikunuro rwake,
\v	8	(nokutirudzikunuro rwemweya weupenyu wavo rwunokosha, uye rwunopera nekusingaperi),
\v	9	kutiarambe ari mupenyu nekusingaperi, asaona kuora.
\v	10	Nokuti anoona kuti vachenjeri vanofa, benzi neasina njere vanoparara pamwe, uye vasiira vamwe fuma yavo.
\v	11	Murangariro wavo wechemukati ndiwo kuti dzimba dzavo dzive dzekusingaperi, nzvimbo dzavo dzekugara dzive dzemazera ose; vanotumidza nyika zhinji mazita avo.
\v	12	Asi munhu ane rukudzo haangagari; anofanana nemhuka dzinoguma.
\v	13	Iyi nzira yavo upenzi hwavo; zvakadaro vanovatevera vanofara nemuromo wavo. Sera.
\p
\v	14	Semakwai vakatarirwa guva, rufu rwuchavafudza; uye vakarurama vachavatonga mangwanani; chimiro chavo ndechekupedzwa neguva, kuti vasava nenzvimbo yekugara.
\v	15	Asi Mwari achadzikinura mweya weupenyu wangu kubva pasimba reguva, nokuti achandigamuchira. Sera.
\v	16	Usatya kana munhu achifumiswa, kana kukudzwa kweimba yake kuchiwedzerwa.
\v	17	Nokuti pakufa haangatakuri chinhu; kukudzwa kwake hakungaburuki kuchimutevera.
\v	18	Kunyange paupenyu hwake airumbidza mweya weupenyu wake, uye vakakurumbidza nokuti unozviitira zvakanaka,
\v	19	achaenda kuzera remadzibaba ake; havangaoni chiedza kusvika pakusingaperi.
\p
\v	20	Munhu anokudzwa, uye asinganzwisisi, wakafanana nemhuka dzinoparara.
\c	5
\s	Dhavhidhi anokumbira kuti afambiswe zvakanaka pakati pevavengi vake
\p
\v	1	Ipainzeve kumashoko angu, Jehovha, mucherekedze kuzvidya moyo kwangu.
\v	2	Teereraikuinzwi rekuchema kwangu, mambo wangu naMwari wangu; nokuti kwamuri ndinonyengetera.
\v	3	Muchanzwainzwi rangu mangwanani, Jehovha; mangwanani ndichakurongedzerai  munyengetero wangu, ndichirindira.
\v	4	Nokutihamusi Mwari anofara muzvakaipa; wakaipa haangagari nemwi.
\v	5	Vanozvikudzahavangazvimisi pamberi pemeso enyu; munovenga vose vaiti vezvakaipa.
\v	6	Muchaparadzavanotaura nhema. Jehovha anosema munhu weropa neunyengeri.
\v	7	Asikana ndiri ini, ndichapinda muimba yenyu mukuwanda kwengoni dzenyu; ndichashumira ndakananga kutembere yenyu tsvene mukukutyai.
\v	8	Nditungamirirei,Jehovha, mukururama kwenyu nekuda kwevavengi vangu; ruramisai nzira yenyu pamberi pangu.
\v	9	Nokutihapana uchokwadi pamuromo wavo; mukati mavo uipi; huro yavo iguva rakashama; vanobata kumeso nerurimi rwavo.
\v	10	Revai kuti vane mhosva, Mwari. Ngavawe nemano avo; muvarase nekuda kweuwandu hwezvitadzo zvavo, nokuti vakakumukirai.
\v	11	Asi ngavafare vose vanovimba nemwi; ngavadanidzire nguva dzose nemufaro, nokuti munovadzivirira; nevanoda zita renyu ngavafare mamuri.
\v	12	Nokuti imwi Jehovha mucharopafadza wakarurama; muchamukomberedza nenyasha senhovo huru.
\c	50
\s	Kushumira Mwari kwechokwadi
\p
\v	1	Mwariwevamwari, Jehovha, wakataura, nekudana nyika kubva pakubuda kwezuva kusvika pakuvira kwaro.
\v	2	ArimuZiyoni, kuperera kwekunaka, Mwari wakapenya.
\v	3	Mwariwedu achauya, uye haanganyarari; moto pamberi pake uchaparadza; uye kuchava nedutu guru remhepo kumativi ake ose.
\v	4	Achadanakumatenga ari kumusoro, nepanyika, kutonga vanhu vake.
\v	5	Unganidziraivatsvene vangu kwandiri, avo vakaita sungano neni nechibairo.
\v	6	Zvinomatenga achaparidza kururama kwake, nokuti Mwari mutongi amene. Sera.
\v	7	Inzwai,vanhu vangu, zvino ndichataura; Israeri, zvino ndichakupupurira; ndini Mwari, Mwari wako.
\v	8	Handingakumhurinekuda kwezvibairo zvako, kana zvipo zvako zvinopiswa zvinogara pamberi pangu.
\v	9	Handingatorinzombe diki kubva paimba yako,  kana nhongo dzembudzi kubva pazvirugu zvako.
\v	10	Nokuti mhuka imwe neimwe yesango ndeyangu, mombe zhinji pamakomo ane churu.
\v	11	Ndinoziva shiri imwe neimwe yemakomo, nemhuka dzesango dzineni.
\v	12	Kana ndaiva nenzara, handizaikuudza, nokuti nyika ndeyangu, nekuzara kwayo.
\v	13	Ndingadya nyama yehando here, kana kunwa ropa rembudzi?
\v	14	Bairai kuna Mwari chibairo chekuvonga, uye zadzisa mhiko dzako kuna Wekumusoro-soro.
\v	15	Uye dana kwandiri pazuva redambudziko. Ndichakununura ugondirumbidza.
\p
\v	16	Asi kune wakaipa Mwari anoti: Unei nazvo kuti urondedzere zvimiso zvangu, kuti utore sungano yangu pamuromo wako?
\v	17	Iwe zvaunovenga kurairwa, nekurasira mashoko angu shure kwako.
\v	18	Kana uchiona mbavha, unofarirana nayo; nemugove wako uri pamhombwe.
\v	19	Unotuma muromo wako kune zvakaipa, nerurimi rwako rwunobatanidza unyengeri.
\v	20	Unogara, uchitaura kurwisa hama yako; unopa mhosva mwanakomana wamai vako.
\v	21	Wakaita izvi ndikanyarara; wakafunga kuti ndakangofanana newe; ndakakutsiura, ndikakurongedzera pamberi pemeso ako.
\v	22	Cherekedzai henyu izvi, imwi munokanganwa Mwari, zvimwe ndibvamburanye kukasava nemununuri.
\v	23	Anopa chipo chekuvonga anondirumbidza; neanogadzira nzira  yake ndichamuratidza ruponeso rwaMwari.
\c	51
\s	Rwiyo rwekuchema zvivi
\p
\v	1	Ndinzwireitsitsi, Mwari, zvichienderana nerudo rweunyoro hwenyu; zvichienderana neuwandu hwengoni dzenyu, dzimai zvitadzo zvangu.
\v	2	Ndisukeikwazvo kubva pauipi hwangu, uye ndinatsei kubva pachivi changu.
\v	3	Nokutizvitadzo zvangu ini ndinoziva, uye chivi changu chinogara chiri pamberi pangu.
\p
\v	4	Ndakatadzakwamuri, kwamuri moga, uye ndakaita chakaipa pameso penyu; kuti kunzi makarurama pakutaura kwenyu, makachena pakutonga kwenyu.
\v	5	Tarirai,ndakaberekerwa muuipi; uye mai vangu vakagamuchira nhumbu yangu muzvivi.
\v	6	Tariraimunoda chokwadi mune zvemukati; nepakavanda munondizivisa uchenjeri.
\p
\v	7	Ndinatseinehisopi, zvino ndichava wakachena; ndishambidzei, zvino ndichava wakachena kupfuura magada echando.
\v	8	Ndinzwiseimufaro nekupembera,  kuti mapfupa  amakavhuna afare.
\v	9	Vanzaichiso chenyu kubva pazvivi zvangu, uye dzimai zvakaipa zvangu zvose.
\v	10	Ndisikirei moyo wakachena, Mwari; uye vandudzai mukati mangu mweya wakasimba.
\v	11	Regai kundirasa kubva pachiso chenyu; uye musabvisa mweya wenyu mutsvene kwandiri.
\v	12	Dzoserai kwandiri mufaro weruponeso rwenyu, uye nditsigirei  nemweya unoda.
\v	13	 Ipapo ndichadzidzisa vadariki nzira dzenyu; uye vatadzi vachatendeukira kwamuri.
\p
\v	14	Ndinunurei pamhosva yeropa, Mwari, Mwari weruponeso rwangu; rurimi rwangu ruchaimbira kururama kwenyu zvikuru.
\v	15	Ishe, zarurai miromo yangu; zvino muromo wangu uchaparidza rumbidzo yenyu.
\v	16	Nokuti hamudi chibairo; nokuti ndingadai ndapa; hamufariri chipo chinopiswa.
\v	17	Zvibairo zvaMwari mweya wakaputsika; moyo wakaputsika newakapwanyika, Mwari, hamungashori.
\p
\v	18	Itirai Ziyoni zvakanaka mukuda kwenyu; vakai masvingo eJerusarema.
\v	19	Ipapo muchafadzwa nezvibairo zvekururama, nechipo chinopiswa, nechipo chose chinopiswa; ipapo vachapa nzombe zhinji pamusoro pearitari yenyu.
\c	52
\s	Kushaya maturo kwekuzvikudza nekuita zvakaipa
\p
\v	1	Unozvirumbidzireinezvakaipa, mhare? Tsitsi dzaMwari  dziripo mazuva ose.
\v	2	Rurimirwako runoronga kuparadza kukuru, sechisvo chinopinza, rwunoita unyengeri.
\v	3	Unodazvakaipa kupfuura zvakanaka, nhema kupfuura kutaura zvakarurama. Sera.
\v	4	Unodamashoko ose ekuparadza, rurimi rwunonyengera.
\v	5	SaizvozvoMwari achakuputsa nekusingaperi; achakubata akubvise, akuvhomore kubva patende, nekukudzura kubva panyika yevapenyu. Sera.
\p
\v	6	Zvinovakarurama vachaona uye vachatya, uye vachamuseka,  vachiti:
\v	7	Tarirai,munhu asina kuita Mwari nhare yake, asi wakavimba neuwandu hwefuma yake; akasimba muuipi hwake.
\v	8	Asiini ndakaita semuorivhi munyoro muimba yaMwari; ndakavimba netsitsi dzaMwari nekusingaperi-peri.
\v	9	Ndichakuvongainekusingaperi, nokuti maka zviita; uye ndichamirira zita renyu nokuti rakanaka pamberi pevatsvene venyu.
\c	53
\s	Vanhu vose vakashata
\p
\v	1	Benzirakati mumoyo maro: Hakuna Mwari. Vakaodza, vakaita uipi hunonyangadza; hakuna anoita zvakanaka.
\v	2	Mwariwakatarisa pasi ari kumatenga pamusoro pevanakomana vevanhu, kuona kana pane anonzwisisa, anotsvaka Mwari.
\v	3	Umweneumwe wavo wakadzokera shure; vakasvibiswa pamwe chete; hakuna anoita zvakanaka, hakuna neumwe.
\v	4	Vaitivezvakaipa havana zivo here? Avo vanodya vanhu vangu  sevanodya chingwa. Havadani Mwari.
\v	5	Ipapovaitya zvekutya, pasina chinotyisa; nokuti Mwari wakaparadzira mapfupa eanokudzikirai musasa; maka vanyadzisa; nokuti Mwari wakavazvidza.
\p
\v	6	Dairuponeso rukuru rwaIsraeri rwaibva paZiyoni! Mwari paanodzosa utapwa hwevanhu vake, Jakove achafara, Israeri achapembera.
\c	54
\s	Dhavhidhi anonyengetera kuti anunurwe pavavengi vake
\p
\v	1	Mwari,ndiponesei nezita renyu, uye nditongei nesimba renyu.
\v	2	Mwari,inzwai munyengetero wangu; ipai nzeve pamashoko emuromo wangu.
\v	3	Nokutivatorwa vandimukira, uye vamanikidzi vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu. Havana kuisa Mwari pamberi pavo. Sera.
\p
\v	4	Tarirai,Mwari mubatsiri wangu. Ishe ari pane vanotsigira mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	5	Achatsivauipi kuvavengi vangu; vapedzei muchokwadi chenyu.
\v	6	Ndichakubairaichipo nekuzvidira; ndicharumbidza zita renyu, Jehovha, nokuti rakanaka.
\v	7	Nokutiwakandinunura kubva mudambudziko rose; uye ziso rangu rakaona  chishuwo changu pavavengi vangu.
\c	55
\s	Dhavhidhi anochema pakutambudzika kwake
\p
\v	1	Ipainzeve, Mwari, kumunyengetero wangu, uye musazvivanza pamukumbiro wangu.
\v	2	Teereraikwandiri, uye ndipindurei. Ndinodzungaira mukuchema kwangu, ndinoita rukunga;
\v	3	nekudakweinzwi remuvengi, nekuda kwemanikidzo yewakaipa; nokuti vakandiwisira zvakaipa, uye vanondivenga nehasha.
\v	4	Moyowangu unorwadziswa kwazvo mukati mangu; uye magarudzo erufu akandiwira.
\v	5	Kuvhundukanekubvunda zvakandisvikira; uye kutya kukuru kwakandifukidza.
\v	6	Zvinondakati: Dai ndaiva nemapapiro senjiva! Ndaibhururukira kure, ndikanozorora.
\v	7	Tarirai,ndaitizira kure ndikanogara murenje. Sera.
\v	8	Ndaikurumidzakupukunyuka kwangu kubva pamhepo inovhuvhuta, kubva padutu guru remhepo.
\p
\v	9	Paradzai,Ishe, paradzanisai rurimi rwavo, nokuti ndakaona manikidzo negakava muguta.
\v	10	Masikati neusiku vanoripoteredza pamasvingo aro; uye uipi nedambudziko zviri pakati paro.
\v	11	Uipi huri mukati maro; uye manikidzo neunyengeri hazvibvi mumugwagwa waro.
\v	12	Nokuti haasi muvengi wakandishora; dai zvakadaro ndaizvitakura; haasi anondivenga anozvikudza pamusoro pangu; kana zvakadaro ndaimuvanda.
\v	13	Asi ndiwe, munhu wakaenzana neni, shamwari yangu nemuzikanwi wangu.
\v	14	Tairairana zvinotapira tiri pamwe chete; takaenda muimba yaMwari muchaunga.
\p
\v	15	Rufu ngaruvanyangire; ngavaburukire kugehena vari vapenyu; nokuti zvakaipa zviri munzvimbo dzavo dzekugara, mukati mavo.
\v	16	Kana ndiri ini, ndichadana kuna Mwari; uye Jehovha achandiponesa.
\v	17	Madekwani nemangwanani nemasikati ndichagunun'una ndichiungudza; uye achanzwa inzwi rangu.
\v	18	Wakanunura mweya weupenyu wangu murugare kubva pahondo yekundirwisa; nokuti vaiva pavazhinji vanondipikisa.
\v	19	Mwari achanzwa, achavatambudza, iye aiva agere kare. Sera. Nokuti havana shanduko zhinji, naizvozvo havatyi Mwari.
\v	20	Wakatandavadza maoko ake kurwisa vane rugare naye; wakasvibisa sungano yake.
\v	21	Muromo wake waitedza seruomba, izvo moyo wake ihondo; mashoko ake aiva akanyorova kupfuura mafuta, asi iwo minondo yakavhomorwa.
\p
\v	22	Kanda mutoro wako pamusoro paJehovha, uye iye achakutsigira; haabvumi rinhi narinhi kuti wakarurama azungunuswe.
\v	23	Asi imwi, Mwari, muchavaburusira kugomba rekuparadzwa; vanhu veropa neunyengeri havangararami hafu yemazuva avo. Asi ini ndichavimba nemwi.
\c	56
\s	Kuvimba naMwari
\p
\v	1	Ndinzwireitsitsi, Mwari, nokuti munhu anondimedza; zuva rose achirwa anondimanikidza.
\v	2	Vavengivangu vano ndimedza zuva rose; nokuti vanondirwisa nekuzvikudza vazhinji.
\p
\v	3	Zuvarandinotya, ini ndichavimba nemwi.
\v	4	MunaMwari ndicharumbidza shoko rake; muna Mwari ndinovimba, handingatyi. Nyama ingandiitei?
\p
\v	5	Zuvarose vanoshonyorora mashoko angu; mifungo yavo yose inondirwisa nezvakaipa.
\v	6	Vanoungana,vanovanda, vanochenjerera nhanho dzangu, kana vachirindira mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	7	Vachapukunyukanezvakaipa here? Mukutsamwa wisirai vanhu pasi, Mwari.
\p
\v	8	Makaverengakudzungaira kwangu; imwi isai misodzi yangu muhombodo yenyu; haimo murugwaro rwenyu here?
\v	9	Ipapovavengi vangu vachadzokera shure nezuva randinodana. Ndinoziva izvi kuti Mwari ari kwandiri.
\v	10	Muna Mwari ndicharumbidza shoko; muna Jehovha ndicharumbidza shoko.
\v	11	Muna Mwari ndinovimba; handingatyi; munhu angandiitei?
\p
\v	12	Mhiko dzenyu dziri pamusoro pangu, Mwari; ndichadzosa rumbidzo huru kwamuri.
\v	13	Nokuti makanunura mweya weupenyu wangu kubva parufu, hongu, tsoka dzangu pakugumburwa; kuti ndifambe pamberi paMwari muchiedza chevapenyu.
\c	57
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kununurwa
\p
\v	1	Ndinzwireitsitsi, Mwari, ndinzwirei tsitsi; nokuti mweya weupenyu wangu unovimba nemwi; uye ndichatizira kumumvuri wemapapiro enyu, kusvika mharadzo dzapfuura.
\v	2	Ndichachemakuna Mwari Wekumusoro-soro, kuna Mwari anondizadzisira.
\v	3	Achatumaari kumatenga, ndokundiponesa, anonyomba anondimedza. Sera. Mwari achatuma tsitsi dzake nechokwadi chake.
\p
\v	4	Mweyaweupenyu wangu uri pakati peshumba; ndinorara pakati pevanopfuta, vanakomana vevanhu, mazino avo mapfumo nemiseve, uye rurimi rwavo munondo unopinza.
\v	5	Ivaimakakwirira kumusoro kwekumatenga, Mwari; kubwinya kwenyu ngakuve pamusoro penyika yose.
\v	6	Vakagadziriratsoka dzangu mumbure; mweya weupenyu wangu wakakotama; vakachera gomba pamberi pangu; vakawira mukati maro. Sera.
\p
\v	7	Moyowangu wakasimba, Mwari, moyo wangu wakasimba; ndichaimba, zvirokwazvo, ndichaimba ndipe rumbidzo.
\v	8	Mukaiwe, rukudzo rwangu; muka iwe, mutengeranwa nembira! Ndichamuka mangwanani.
\v	9	Ndichakurumbidzaipakati pevanhu, Ishe. Ndichaimba kwamuri pakati pevahedheni.
\v	10	Nokuti tsitsi dzenyu ihuru kusvika kumatenga, nekutendeka kwenyu kusvika kumakore.
\v	11	Ivai makakwirira kumusoro kwekumatenga, Mwari; kubwinya kwenyu ngakuve pamusoro penyika yose.
\c	58
\s	Kukumbira kuti vakaipa vaparadzwe
\p
\v	1	Zvirokwazvomunotaura zvakarurama here, imwi vatongi? Munotonga zvakarurama here, imwi vanakomana vevanhu?
\v	2	Hongu,mumoyo munoita zvakaipa; munoyerera manikidzo yemaoko enyu panyika.
\v	3	Vakaipavakava vatorwa kubva muchibereko; vanotsauka kubva muchizvaro, vachitaura nhema.
\v	4	Uturuhwavo hwakafanana neuturu hwenyoka; vakafanana nechiva chisinganzwi, chinodzivira nzeve yacho,
\v	5	chisingateereriinzwi revazevezeri, mukwezvi nyanzvi yeukwezvi.
\p
\v	6	Mwari,vhunai mazino avo mumuromo mavo; Jehovha, gurai mazino pashaya yeshumbahono diki.
\v	7	Ngavanyungudukesemvura inoyerera; kana achishumba  gangauta kufura miseve yake, ngaive seyakagurika.
\v	8	Sehozhwainonyunguduka ngavafambe;  segavamwedzi remukadzi ngavasaona zuva.
\v	9	Haridzenyu dzisati dzanzwa huni dzeminzwa, acha vapeperesa semuchamupupuri sevapenyu sehasha.
\p
\v	10	Wakarurama achafara paachaona tsivo; achashambidza tsoka dzake muropa rewakaipa.
\v	11	Kuti munhu ati: Zvirokwazvo kune mubairo wewakarurama; zvirokwazvo ndiMwari anotonga panyika.
\c	59
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kununurwa pavavengi
\p
\v	1	Ndinunureipavavengi vangu, Mwari wangu; ndiise pakakwirira kubva pane vanondimukira.
\v	2	Ndinunureikubva kuvaiti vezvakaipa, uye ndiponesei pavanhu veropa.
\p
\v	3	Nokutitarirai, vanovandira mweya weupenyu wangu; vane simba vakaunganira kundirwisa, pasina chitadzo changu uye pasina chivi changu, Jehovha.
\v	4	Vanomhanyanekuzvigadzirira pasina mhosva; mukai, mundibatsire, muone.
\v	5	Naizvozvoimwi Jehovha Mwari wedzihondo, Mwari waIsraeri, mukai kuti mushanyire vahedheni vose; musanzwira tsitsi umwe wevanyengeri pauipi. Sera.
\v	6	Vanodzokamadekwani, vanoita kuhuhudza seimbwa, ndokupoteredza guta.
\v	7	Tarirai,vanodzvova nemiromo yavo, minondo iri pamiromo yavo, nokuti  vanoti: Ndiani anonzwa?
\v	8	Asiimwi Jehovha muchavaseka, muchatuka vahedheni vose.
\v	9	Nekuda kwesimba rake ndichakurindirai; nokuti Mwari inhare yangu.
\v	10	Mwari wengoni dzangu achanditangira; Mwari achandionesa  chishuwo changu pavavengi vangu.
\v	11	Musavauraya, zvimwe vanhu vekwedu vakanganwe; vadzungaidzei nesimba renyu, uye muvaburusire pasi, imwi Jehovha, nhovo yedu.
\v	12	 Nechivi chemuromo wavo,  neshoko remiromo yavo, ngavabatwe pakuzvikudza kwavo, uye nekuda kwekunyomba nekutaura nhema  dzavanorondedzera.
\v	13	 Vapedzei muhasha,  vapedzei vasavapo, kuti vazive kuti Mwari anotonga kwaJakove kusvika kumigumo yenyika. Sera.
\v	14	Zvino ngavadzoke pamadekwani, ngavahuhudze seimbwa, uye vapoteredze guta.
\v	15	Ngavadzungairire kudya; kana vasina kuguta ngavapedze usiku  vachidaro.
\p
\v	16	Asi ini ndichaimbira simba renyu; hongu ndichaimbira tsitsi dzenyu zvikuru mangwanani, nokuti manga muri nhare yangu neutiziro pazuva rekutambudzika kwangu.
\v	17	Ndichakuimbirai nziyo dzekurumbidza, imwi simba rangu; nokuti Mwari ndiye nhare yangu yakakwirira, Mwari wetsitsi dzangu.
\c	6
\s	Dhavhidhi anochema zvivi zvake
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,musanditsiura pakutsamwa kwenyu, musandiranga nehasha dzenyu.
\v	2	Ndinzwireitsitsi, Jehovha, nokuti handina simba; ndiporesei, Jehovha, nokuti mapfupa angu anoshungurudzika.
\v	3	Nemweyaweupenyu wangu unoshungurudzika kwazvo. Asi imwi Jehovha, kusvika rinhi?
\v	4	Dzokai,Jehovha, nunurai mweya weupenyu wangu; mundiponese nekuda kwetsitsi dzenyu.
\v	5	Nokutiparufu hapana kukurangarirai; muguva ndiani angakuvongai?
\v	6	Ndanetanekugomera kwangu; usiku hwose ndinoshambirisa nhovo yangu; ndinonyorovedza mubhedha wangu nemisodzi yangu.
\v	7	Zisorangu radyiwa nekuda kwedambudziko, rinosakara nekuda kwevadzivisi vangu vose.
\p
\v	8	Ibvaikwandiri imwi mose vaiti vezvakaipa. Nokuti Jehovha wakanzwa inzwi rekurira kwangu.
\v	9	Jehovhawakanzwa mukumbiro wangu; Jehovha achagamuchira munyengetero wangu.
\v	10	Vavengi vangu vose vachanyadzwa nekuvhunduswa kwazvo; vachadzoka, vachanyadziswa mukubwaira kweziso.
\c	60
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kubatsirwa nekukunda
\p
\v	1	Mwari,manga makatirasa, makatiputikira; makatsamwa; dzokerai kwatiri.
\v	2	Makabvundisanyika; makaitsemura; poresai mitswe yayo; nokuti inozununguka.
\v	3	Makaratidzavanhu venyu zvakaoma; makatinwisa waini yekudzadzarika.
\v	4	Makapamureza kune vanokutyai, kuti usimudzwe nekuda kwechokwadi. Sera.
\v	5	Kutivadikanwi venyu vanunurwe; ponesai  neruoko rwenyu rwerudyi, uye ndipindurei.
\p
\v	6	Mwariwakataura pautsvene hwake. Ndichapembera; ndichagova Shekemu, uye ndichayera mupata weSukoti.
\v	7	Giriyadhinderangu, uye Manase ndewangu; Efuremuwo inhare yemusoro wangu; Judha mupi wangu wemurau.
\v	8	Moabhumudziyo wangu wekushambira; pamusoro peEdhomu ndichakandira shangu yangu; Firisitia, pururudza nekukunda nekuda kwangu.
\p
\v	9	Ndianiachandiisa  muguta rakasimba? Ndiani achanditungamirira kuEdhomu?
\v	10	Hamuna kutirasa here, Mwari, uye hamubudi, Mwari, nedzihondo dzedu?
\v	11	Tipei rubatsiro padambudziko, nokuti ruponeso rwemunhu harwuna maturo.
\v	12	Muna Mwari tichaita neumhare, nokuti ndiye achatsikira vavengi vedu pasi.
\c	61
\s	Dhavhidhi anovimba naMwari pakutambudzika kwake
\p
\v	1	Inzwai,Mwari, kuchema kwangu; teererai kumunyengetero wangu.
\p
\v	2	Ndichadanakwamuri ndiri pamugumo wepanyika, kana moyo wangu wopera; nditungamirirei kudombo rakakwirira kundidarika.
\v	3	Nokutimanga muri utiziro hwangu, shongwe yakasimba kubva pamuvengi.
\v	4	Ndichagaramutende renyu rinhi narinhi; ndichatizira kunzvimbo yekuvanda yemapapiro enyu. Sera.
\v	5	Nokutiimwi Mwari, makanzwa mhiko dzangu; maka ndipa nhaka yeavo vanotya zita renyu.
\v	6	Muchawedzeramazuva pamazuva amambo; makore ake achava sezera nezera.
\v	7	Achagarapamberi paMwari rinhi narinhi; mugadze ngoni nechokwadi  kuti zvimuchengete.
\p
\v	8	Naizvozvondichaimbira zita renyu rumbidzo kusvika rinhi narinhi, kuti ndizadzise mhiko dzangu zuva  nezuva.
\c	62
\s	Kunyarara kwemweya wemunhu anovimba naMwari
\p
\v	1	Zvirokwazvo,mweya weupenyu wangu unorindira Mwari murunyararo; ruponeso rwangu rwunobva kwaari.
\v	2	Ndiyeoga dombo rangu, neruponeso rwangu, shongwe yangu; handingazununguswi zvikuru.
\p
\v	3	Kusvikarinhi muchindirongera zvakaipa nemunhu? Mose muchaurawa, serusvingo rwakarereka, ruzhowa rwunotsveyama.
\v	4	Vanorongakoga ku musunda kubva kuukuru hwake; vanofarira nhema; nemuromo wavo vanoropafadza, asi mukati mavo vanotuka. Sera.
\p
\v	5	Mweyaweupenyu wangu, rindira Mwari koga murunyararo, nokuti tariro yangu inobva kwaari.
\v	6	Ndiyeoga dombo rangu, neruponeso rwangu, shongwe yangu; handingazununguswi.
\v	7	Ruponesorwangu nerukudzo rwangu zviri kuna Mwari; dombo resimba rangu, utiziro hwangu, zviri kuna Mwari.
\v	8	Vimbainaye nenguva dzose, vanhu; dururai moyo wenyu pamberi pake; Mwari ndiye utiziro hwedu. Sera.
\p
\v	9	Zvirokwazvovanakomana vevanhu hachisi chinhu, vanakomana vemunhu unyepi; pazviyero vakareruka kupfuura zvisina maturo pamwe chete.
\v	10	Regai kuvimba nemanikidzo, uye musamisa tariro isina maturo paupambi; kana fuma ichiwanda, musaisa moyo  pairi.
\p
\v	11	Mwari wakataura kamwe, ndakanzwa izvi kaviri, kuti simba nderaMwari.
\v	12	Netsitsiwo ndedzenyu, Ishe; nokuti imwi munoripira umwe neumwe zvichienderana nebasa rake.
\c	63
\s	Dhavhidhi anoshuva Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Mwari,muri Mwari wangu, ndichakutsvakai mangwanani; mweya weupenyu wangu unenyota kwamuri, nyama yangu inokushuvai, panyika yakaoma, yakasakara, isina mvura.
\v	2	Naizvozvondakatarira kwamuri panzvimbo tsvene, kuti ndione simba renyu nekubwinya kwenyu.
\v	3	Nokutirudo rweunyoro hwenyu rwuri nani pane upenyu; miromo yangu ichakurumbidzai.
\v	4	Saizvozvondichakurumbidzai ndichiri mupenyu; ndichasimudza maoko angu muzita renyu.
\v	5	Mweyaweupenyu wangu uchaguta nezvinenge mafuta nezvakakora; uye muromo wangu ucharumbidza nemiromo inofadza.
\v	6	Kanandichikurangarirai panhovo yangu, pazvirindo ndinokufungai.
\v	7	Nokutimanga muri rubatsiro rwangu; naizvozvo pamumvuri wemapapiro enyu ndichaimba ndifare.
\v	8	Mweyaweupenyu wangu unonamatira shure kwenyu; ruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwunonditsigira.
\v	9	Asiavo, vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu kuparadza, vachaenda munzvimbo dzepasi dzenyika.
\v	10	Vachakumikidzwa kusimba remunondo; vachava mugove wemakava.
\v	11	Asi mambo achafara muna Mwari; umwe neumwe anopika naye achazvikudza; asi muromo wevanoreva nhema uchadzivirwa.
\c	64
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira kudzivirirwa pavavengi
\p
\v	1	Inzwaiinzwi rangu, Mwari, pachichemo changu; chengetedzai upenyu hwangu pakutya muvengi.
\v	2	Ndivanzeipazano rakavanda revakaipa, pabope revaiti vezvakaipa,
\v	3	vakarodzarurimi rwavo semunondo, vakashumba museve wavo,  iro shoko rinovava,
\v	4	kufurawakarurama vari panzvimbo dzakavanda; kamwe-kamwe vanomufura, uye vasingatyi.
\v	5	Vanozvisimbisa panyaya yakaipa; vanorondedzera zvekuteya misungo pakavanda; vanoti: Ndiani angaiona?
\v	6	Vanotsvakisisazvitadzo;  vanoti: Tagadzirira nezano rakavanzwa neunyengeri; mufungo wemunhu wechemukati pamwe nemoyo zvakadzika.
\p
\v	7	AsiMwari achavafura  nemuseve; mavanga avo achakurumidza.
\v	8	Zvinovanogumbusa rurimi rwavo pamusoro pavo; vose vanovaona vachatiza.
\v	9	Zvinovanhu vose vachatya; uye vachaparidza basa raMwari; uye kuita kwake vachicherekedza.
\v	10	Wakarurama achafara muna Jehovha, uye achavimba naye; uye vose vakarurama pamoyo vachazvikudza.
\c	65
\s	Dhavhidhi anorumbidza Mwari
\p
\v	1	Kumiriramurunyararo irumbidzo kwamuri, Mwari, paZiyoni; uye mhiko dzichazadziswa mamuri.
\v	2	Munzwiwemunyengetero, nyama yose ichauya kwamuri.
\v	3	Zvinhuzveuipi zvandikunda; zvitadzo zvedu, imwi muchazviitira chiyananiso.
\v	4	Wakaropafadzwa wamunosarudza uye  wamunoswededza kuti agare pavazhe dzenyu; tichagutiswa neunaku hweimba yenyu, tembere yenyu tsvene.
\v	5	Mukururamamunotipindura zvinhu zvinotyisa, Mwari weruponeso rwedu, tariro yemigumo yose yenyika, neye vari kure  kugungwa.
\v	6	Anomisamakomo nekugwinya kwake, akasunga chiuno nesimba.
\v	7	Anonyaradzakutinhira kwemakungwa, iko kutinhira kwemafungu awo, nebope revanhu.
\v	8	Naivovagere kumigumo vanotya zviratidzo zvenyu; munoimbisa mangwanani nemadekwani nemufaro.
\p
\v	9	Munoshanyiranyika nekuidiridza; munoifumisa zvikuru; rwizi rwaMwari ruzere nemvura; munovagadzirira zviyo, kana maigadzira saizvozvo.
\v	10	Munodiridza mihoronga yayo kwazvo; munoenzanisa mipanje yayo; munoinyorovesa nekupfunha; munoropafadza kumera kwayo.
\v	11	Munoshongedza mwaka nekorona yeunaku hwenyu; uye makwara enyu anodonha mafuta.
\v	12	Anodonhera pamafuro erenje; nezvikomo zvinozvisunga nemufaro.
\v	13	Mafuro akapfekedzwa mapoka ezvipfuwo; uye mipata yakafukidzwa nezviyo; zvinopururudza, uye zvinoimba.
\c	66
\s	Kurumbidza Mwari nekumuvonga
\p
\v	1	Pururudzaikuna Mwari, imwi nyika yose.
\v	2	Imbiraikubwinya kwezita rake; muite rukudzo rwake rwuve nekubwinya.
\v	3	Itiikuna Mwari: Mabasa enyu anotyisa sei! Kubudikidza neukuru hwesimba renyu vavengi venyu vachazviisa pasi penyu neunyengeri.
\v	4	Nyikayose ichakushumirai, uye ichakuimbirai; ichaimba zita renyu. Sera.
\p
\v	5	Uyaimuone mabasa aMwari; anotyisa pakuita kuvana vevanhu.
\v	6	Anoshanduragungwa kuva nyika yakaoma; vakayambuka rwizi netsoka. Ipapo takafara maari.
\v	7	Anotonganesimba rake rinhi narinhi; meso ake anorinda marudzi; vapanduki ngavarege kuzvikudza. Sera.
\p
\v	8	VongaiMwari wedu, marudzi, uye munzwise inzwi rerumbidzo yake.
\v	9	Iyewakaisa mweya weupenyu wedu muupenyu, uye asina kubvuma kuti tsoka yedu itedzemuke.
\v	10	Nokuti makatiedza, Mwari; makatinatsa sekunatswa kwesirivha.
\v	11	Makatipinza mumumbure; makaisa dambudziko pazviuno zvedu.
\v	12	Makatasvisa munhu pamusoro pemusoro wedu; takapinda nemumoto nemumvura; asi makatibudisira kunzvimbo ine zvakawanda.
\p
\v	13	Ndichapinda mumba menyu nezvipo zvinopiswa; ndichakuripirai mhiko dzangu;
\v	14	miromo yangu dzayakareva, uye muromo wangu dzawakataura ndiri mudambudziko.
\v	15	Ndichapa kwamuri zvibairo zvinopiswa zvezvakakora, nezvipfungaidzo zvinonhuhwira zvemakondohwe; ndichapa nzombe pamwe nembudzi zhinji. Sera.
\p
\v	16	Uyai munzwe, imwi mose munotya Mwari, zvino ndicharondedzera zvaakaitira mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	17	Ndakachema kwaari  nemuromo wangu, zvino akakudzwa pasi perurimi rwangu.
\v	18	Kana ndaitarisa uipi mumoyo mangu, Ishe haazaindinzwa.
\v	19	Zvirokwazvo Mwari wakanzwa; wakateerera kuinzwi remunyengetero wangu.
\p
\v	20	Ngaavongwe Mwari, iye asina kutsausa munyengetero wangu, kana tsitsi yake kubva kwandiri.
\c	67
\s	Rwiyo rwekuvonga
\p
\v	1	Mwaringaave netsitsi kwatiri, uye atiropafadze; ngaavhenekerese chiso chake patiri. Sera.
\v	2	Kutinzira yenyu izikanwe panyika, ruponeso rwenyu pakati pemarudzi ose.
\p
\v	3	Marudzingaakurumbidzei, Mwari; marudzi ose ngaakurumbidzei.
\v	4	Marudzingaafare uye aimbe nekupembera nokuti muchatonga vanhu zvakarurama; uye munotungamirira marudzi panyika. Sera.
