\v	5	Marudzingaakurumbidzei, Mwari; marudzi ose ngaakurumbidzei.
\p
\v	6	Nyikaichabereka zvibereko zvayo; Mwari, Mwari wedu achatiropafadza.
\v	7	Mwariachatiropafadza; uye migumo yose yenyika ichamutya.
\c	68
\s	Rwiyo rwekurumbidza Mwari
\p
\v	1	Mwaringaasimuke; vavengi vake ngavaparadzirwe; uye vanomuvenga ngavatize pamberi pake.
\v	2	Sekupepereswakweutsi,  vapeperesei; sekunyunguduswa kwenamo pamberi pemoto, vakaipa ngavaparare pamberi paMwari.
\v	3	Asivakarurama ngavafare; ngavafarise pamberi paMwari; hongu, ngavafare nemufaro.
\p
\v	4	ImbiraiMwari; imbirai zita rake rumbidzo; musimudzire iye anotasva achipfuura nemurenje nezita rake Jehovha; uye farai pamberi pake.
\v	5	Babavenherera, nemutongi wemhosva dzechirikadzi, Mwari paugaro hwake utsvene.
\v	6	Mwarianovagarisa vari voga mumhuri, anobudisa vakasungwa achivaisa pakubudirira; asi vapanduki vanogara panyika yakaoma.
\p
\v	7	Mwari,pakubuda kwenyu pamberi pevanhu venyu, pakufamba kwenyu murenje; Sera;
\v	8	nyikayakadengenyeka, matenga akanyorovedzawo pamberi paMwari; Sinai iri, pamberi paMwari, Mwari waIsraeri.
\v	9	Makanaisamvura zhinji, Mwari, pamunosimbisa imwi nhaka yenyu yaneta.
\v	10	Ungano yenyu yakagaramo; Mwari, makagadzirira murombo muunaku hwenyu.
\p
\v	11	Ishe wakapa shoko; vakadzi vanokumikidza nyaya vaiva chaunga chikuru.
\v	12	Madzimambo ehondo anotiza, anotiza. Nemukadzi mugari weimba anogova zvakapambiwa.
\v	13	Kunyange muchirara pakati pezvirugu zvemakwai,  muchava semapapiro enjiva akafukidzwa nesirivha, neminhenga yawo negoridhe reruvara rwemashizha akatsvukuruka.
\v	14	Wemasimbaose paanoparadzira madzimambomo, zvakafanana nemagada echando muZarimoni.
\p
\v	15	Gomo raMwari igomo reBhashani; gomo rine mikwidza igomo reBhashani.
\v	16	Munotarisirei negodo, imwi makomo ane mikwidza? Gomo Mwari raakashuvira kuva chigaro chake. Hongu, Jehovha achagara kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	17	Ngoro dzaMwari zvuru makumi maviri, zvuru zvezvuru; Ishe ari pakati padzo, Sinai, panzvimbo tsvene.
\v	18	Makakwira kumusoro; makatapa vatapwa; makagamuchira zvipo pavanhu, hongu vapandukiwo, kuti Jehovha Mwari agare.
\v	19	Ngaavongwe Ishe; anotitakudza mutoro zuva  nezuva; Mwari ruponeso rwedu. Sera.
\p
\v	20	Mwari wedu ndiMwari weruponeso rukuru; uye kuna Jehovha Ishe kune kununura kukuru parufu.
\v	21	Asi Mwari achapwanya musoro wevavengi vake, ganda remusoro rine vhudzi reanofamba muzvivi zvake.
\v	22	Ishe wakati: Ndichavadzosa kubva paBhashani, ndichadzosa panzvimbo dzakadzika dzegungwa.
\v	23	Kuti rutsoka rwako urwunyike muropa revavengi, rurimi rweimbwa dzako mariri.
\p
\v	24	Vakaona midungwe yenyu, Mwari, midungwe yaMwari wangu, Mambo wangu, panzvimbo tsvene.
\v	25	Pamberi paiva nevaimbi, pashure varidzi vemitengeranwa, pakati vasikana vanoridza makandira.
\v	26	Rumbidzai Mwari paungano huru, Jehovha, kubva pachitubu chaIsraeri.
\v	27	Hoyu Bhenjamini mudiki, mutongi wavo, machinda aJudha, dare ravo, machinda aZebhuruni, machinda aNafutari.
\v	28	Mwari wako wakaraira simba rako; simbisai, Mwari, izvo zvamakatiitira.
\v	29	Nekuda kwetembere yenyu paJerusarema madzimambo achakuvigirai chipo.
\v	30	Tsiurai chikara chetsanga, boka rehando, nemhuru dzemarudzi,  kuti vazvininipise nemakobiri esirivha; aparadzire vanhu vanofara muhondo zhinji.
\v	31	Machinda achauya kubva paEgipita. Itiyopiya achatandavadzira maoko ake kuna Mwari nekukurumidza.
\p
\v	32	Imbirai Mwari, imwi ushe uzhinji hwepanyika; imbirai Ishe rumbidzo. Sera.
\v	33	Kune akatasva matenga ematenga ekare; tarirai, anopa neinzwi rake, inzwi rine simba.
\v	34	Ipai Mwari simba; ukuru hwake huri pamusoro paIsraeri, uye simba rake muzvadenga.
\p
\v	35	Mwari  munotyisa panzvimbo dzenyu tsvene; Mwari waIsraeri ndiye anopa vanhu simba nekugwinya. Mwari ngaavongwe.
\c	69
\s	Munyengetero weanotambudzika
\p
\v	1	Ndiponesei,Mwari, nokuti mvura yasvika kumweya weupenyu.
\v	2	Ndinonyuramunhope yakadzika, pasina kumira; ndapinda munzvimbo dzakadzika dzemvura, mafashame paanondifukidza.
\v	3	Ndanetanekuchema kwangu; huro yangu yaoma; meso angu anopera pakumirira Mwari wangu.
\v	4	Vanondivengapasina chikonzero vakawanda kupfuura vhudzi remusoro wangu; vangandiparadza, vavengi vangu venhema, vane simba. Ipapo zvandisina kupamba ndi chadzorera.
\p
\v	5	Mwari,imwi munoziva maererano neupenzi hwangu, uye zvivi zvangu hazvina kuvanzirwa imwi.
\v	6	Vanokumiriraingavarege kunyadziswa nekuda kwangu, Ishe, Jehovha wehondo; vanokutsvakai ngavarege kumhurwa nekuda kwangu, Mwari waIsraeri.
\v	7	Nokutinekuda kwenyu ndakatakura kumhurwa; nyadzi dzakafukidza chiso changu.
\v	8	Ndakavamutorwa kuhama dzangu, nemubvakure kuvana vamai vangu.
\v	9	Nokutikushingairira imba yenyu kwakandidya; nekushorwa kukuru kwevanokushorai kwakawira pamusoro pangu.
\v	10	Zvino ndakachema pakutsanya kwemweya weupenyu wangu, uye kwakava kushorwa kwangu kukuru.
\v	11	Ndakaitawo saga chipfeko changu, ndokuva shumo kwavari.
\v	12	Vanogara pasuwo vanotaura nezvangu; uye  ndakava nziyo dzevanwi vezvinodhaka.
\p
\v	13	Asi ini, munyengetero wangu uri kwamuri, Jehovha,  panguva yenyasha; Mwari, nekuwanda kwetsitsi dzenyu, ndipindurei, nechokwadi cheruponeso rwenyu.
\v	14	Ndinunurei munhope, uye ndirege kunyura; ngandinunurwe pane vanondivenga nekubva muudziku hwemvura zhinji.
\v	15	Fashame remvura rirege kundifukidza; uye udziku hurege kundimedza; negomba rirege kudzivira muromo waro pamusoro pangu.
\v	16	Ndipindurei, Jehovha, nokuti rudo rweunyoro hwenyu rwakanaka; zvichienderana neuwandu hwetsitsi dzenyu, tendeukirai kwandiri.
\v	17	Zvino musavanzira muranda wenyu chiso chenyu; nokuti ndine dambudziko, kurumidzai mundipindure.
\v	18	Swederai kumweya weupenyu wangu; muudzikunure; ndinunurei nekuda kwevavengi vangu.
\p
\v	19	Imwi munoziva kushorwa kwangu, nekunyadziswa kwangu, nekuzvidzwa kwangu; vavengi vangu vose vari pamberi penyu.
\v	20	Kushorwa kwakaputsa moyo wangu; uye ndakarukutika; ndanga ndakarindira tsitsi, asi kwaiva kusina; nevanyaradzi, asi handina ku vawana.
\v	21	Uye vakandipa nduru kuva zvekudya zvangu; uye pakunzwa nyota kwangu vakandinwisa vhiniga.
\v	22	Tafura yavo ngaive musungo pamberi pavo, uye ive riva revakagarika.
\v	23	Meso avo ngaasvibiriswe kuti  varege kuona; uye murambe muchigudairisa zviuno zvavo.
\v	24	Dururai kutsamwa kwenyu pamusoro pavo; nehasha dzenyu dzinopfuta ngadzivabate.
\v	25	Musasa wavo ngauve dongo; ngakurege kuva neanogara pamatende avo.
\v	26	Nokuti vanodzingirira wamakarova imwi, uye vanorondedzera pamusoro pedambudziko revamakakuvadza.
\v	27	Uye wedzerai kutadza pakutadza kwavo kuti vasapinda pakururama kwenyu.
\v	28	Ngavadzimwe mubhuku revapenyu, uye vasanyorwa pamwe nevakarurama.
\p
\v	29	Asi ini ndiri murombo, ndinoshungurudzika; ruponeso rwenyu, Mwari, ngarwundimise pakakwirira pasingasvikiriki.
\v	30	Ndicharumbidza zita raMwari nerwiyo, uye ndichamukudza nekuvonga.
\v	31	Zvichava zvakanaka kuna Jehovha kupfuura nzombe,  kana hando ine nyanga  nemahwanda.
\v	32	Vanyoro vachaona, vachafara; imwi munotsvaka Mwari, moyo yenyu ichararamawo.
\v	33	Nokuti Jehovha anonzwa vashaiwi, uye haazvidzi vasungwa vake.
\p
\v	34	Matenga nenyika ngazvimurumbidze, makungwa, nezvose zvinopfakanyikamo.
\v	35	Nokuti Mwari achaponesa Ziyoni, nekuvaka maguta aJudha; uye vagaremo ndokuagara nhaka.
\v	36	Uye mbeu yevaranda vake ichaagara nhaka; uye vanoda zita rake vachagara maari.
\c	7
\s	Dhavhidhi anokumbira kuti Jehovha amururamisire
\p
\v	1	JehovhaMwari wangu, ndinovimba nemwi; ndiponesei kune vose vanonditeverera, mundinunure.
\v	2	Zvimweabvambure mweya weupenyu wangu seshumba, abvamburanye pasina anonunura.
\v	3	JehovhaMwari wangu, kana ndakaita izvi; kana mune chakaipa mumaoko angu;
\v	4	kanandakatsiva chakaipa kune waiva nerugare neni (koga ndakapamba ari muvengi wangu pasina chikonzero):
\v	5	Muvengingaateverere mweya weupenyu wangu, aubate; ngaatsikire-tsikire upenyu hwangu pasi; nerukudzo rwangu aise muguruva. Sera.
\p
\v	6	MukaiJehovha, pakutsamwa kwenyu; zvisimudzei nekuda kwehasha dzevavengi vangu, uye mukai nekuda kwangu; makaraira mutongo.
\v	7	Saizvozvoungano yevendudzi ichakupoteredzai; uye dzokerai kumusoro pamusoro payo.
\v	8	Jehovhaanotonga ndudzi; nditongei, Jehovha, zvichienderana nekururama kwangu, uye zvichienderana neuchokwadi hwangu huri mandiri.
\v	9	Haiwa,kuipa kwevakaipa ngakugume, asi simbisai wakarurama; nokuti anoedza moyo netsvo ndiMwari wakarurama.
\p
\v	10	Nhovo yangu iri kuna Mwari, muponesi wevakarurama pamoyo.
\v	11	Mwari mutongi wakarurama, uye ndiMwari anotsamwa pamazuva ose.
\p
\v	12	Kana asingatendeuki, acharodza munondo wake; wakunga uta hwake, ndokuhugadzirira.
\v	13	Wakamugadzirirawo nhumbi dzerufu; anoitira vatevereri vanopisa miseve yake.
\v	14	Tarira, anorwadziwa nemimba yezvakaipa; uye wakava nemimba yezvakashata, ndokubereka nhema.
\v	15	Wakavhukunyura gomba ndokurichera, ndokuwira muhunza yaakaita.
\v	16	Kuipa kwake kuchadzoka pamusoro pemusoro wake, uye kumanikidza kwake kuchaburukira pamusoro panhongonya yake.
\p
\v	17	Ndichavonga Jehovha zvichienderana nekururama kwake; uye ndichaimba rumbidzo kuzita raJehovha Wekumusoro-soro.
\c	70
\s	Dhavhidhi anokumbira kuti Jehovha amurwire
\p
\v	1	Mwari, pakundinunura, Jehovha, kurumidzirai rubatsiro rwangu.
\v	2	Ngavanyadziswevazvidzwe avo vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu; ngavadzoserwe shure vanyadziswe ivo vanofarira dambudziko rangu.
\v	3	Ngavadzokereshure uve mubairo wechinyadzo chavo avo vanoti: Hekani, hekani!
\v	4	Vosevanokutsvakai ngavafare uye vafarisise mamuri; uye vanoda ruponeso rwenyu ngavarambe vachiti: Mwari ngaave mukuru!
\v	5	Asindiri murombo uye mushaiwi; Mwari, kurumidzai kwandiri. Imwi muri rubatsiro rwangu nemununuri wangu; Jehovha, regai kunonoka.
\c	71
\s	Munyengetero wemutana
\p
\v	1	Kwamuri,Jehovha, ndinotizira; ngandirege kunyadziswa kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	2	Ndinunureimukururama kwenyu, uye mundipukunyutse; rerekai nzeve yenyu kwandiri, mugondiponesa.
\v	3	Ivaikwandiri dombo rekugara,  rekupinda nguva nenguva; makapa murairo kundiponesa, nokuti muri dombo rangu nenhare yangu.
\v	4	Mwariwangu, ndinunurei kubva muruoko rwewakaipa, kubva muruoko rweasina kururama neane utsinye.
\p
\v	5	Nokutiimwi muri tariro yangu, Ishe Jehovha, chivimbo changu kubva paudiki hwangu.
\v	6	Ndakazendamapamuri kubva muchizvaro; ndimwi makandibudisa muchibereko chamai vangu; rumbidzo yangu iri kwamuri nguva nenguva.
\v	7	Ndangandiri sechishamiso kuvazhinji; asi imwi muri utiziro hwangu hwakasimba.
\v	8	Muromowangu ngauzadzwe nerumbidzo yenyu, zuva rose nekubwinya kwenyu.
\v	9	Regaikundirasa panguva yekukwegura; musandisiya pakupera kwesimba rangu.
\v	10	Nokuti vavengi vangu vanondireva; nevanovandira mweya weupenyu wangu, vanorangana zano,
\v	11	vachiti: Mwari wamusiya; dzingirirai mumubate, nokuti hakuna mununuri.
\v	12	Mwari, musava kure neni; Mwari wangu, kurumidzirai rubatsiro rwangu.
\v	13	Ngavanyadziswe vapere avo vari vavengi vemweya weupenyu wangu; vanotsvaka kukuvara kwangu ngavafukidzwe nekushorwa nekuzvidzwa.
\v	14	Asi ini ndicharamba ndichivimba, uye ndichawedzera parumbidzo yenyu yose.
\v	15	Muromo wangu ucharondedzera kururama kwenyu, zuva rose ruponeso rwenyu, nokuti handizivi uwandu  hwazvo.
\v	16	Ndichafamba mumasimba aShe Jehovha; ndinotaura kururama kwenyu, kwenyu koga.
\p
\v	17	Mwari, makandidzidzisa kubva paudiki hwangu; uye kusvika ikozvino ndinozivisa zvishamiso zvenyu.
\v	18	Uyewo pandinenge  ndakwegura  ndachena vhudzi, Mwari, musandisiya, kusvika ndazivisa chanza chenyu kuzera, simba renyu kune wose achauya.
\v	19	Kururama kwenyuwo, Mwari, kusvika panhongonya, anoita zvinhu zvikuru, Mwari, ndiani wakaita semwi?
\v	20	Wakandionesa matambudziko mazhinji uye anorwadza, muchandimutsiridzazve, mugondikwidzazve kubva paudziku ukuru hwepasi.
\v	21	Muchawedzera ukuru hwangu, mundinyaradze mativi ose.
\v	22	Neni ndichakurumbidzai nechiridzwa chemutengeranwa, chokwadi chenyu, Mwari wangu; ndichakuimbirai rumbidzo nembira, imwi Mutsvene waIsraeri.
\v	23	Miromo yangu ichapururudza pandichakuimbirai rumbidzo, nemweya weupenyu wangu wamakadzikinura.
\v	24	Nerurimi rwangu rwuchataura zuva rose kururama kwenyu, nokuti vanonyara, nokuti vashoreka, vanotsvaka kukuvara kwangu.
\c	72
\s	Ukuru hwaMambo
\p
\v	1	Mwari,ipai mambo mitongo yenyu, nekururama kwenyu kumwanakomana wamambo.
\v	2	Achatongavanhu venyu nekururama, nevarombo venyu nemutongo wakarurama.
\v	3	Makomoachavigira vanhu rugare, nezvikomo mukururama.
\v	4	Achatongavarombo vevanhu, achaponesa vana vevashaiwi, nekupwanya mumanikidzi.
\v	5	Vachakutyaikana zuva  richingovapo, nemwedzi uchingovapo,  kumazera  nemazera.
\v	6	Achaburukasemvura pauswa hwakaguririrwa, sekunaya kunodiridza pasi.
\v	7	Pamazuvaake wakarurama achatunga, nekuwanda kwerugare, kusvika mwedzi usisipo.
\v	8	Achatongawokubva pagungwa kusvika pagungwa, uye kubva parwizi kusvika pamigumo yenyika.
\v	9	Avovanogara murenje vachafugama pamberi pake; uye vavengi vake vachananzva guruva.
\v	10	Madzimambo eTarishishi neezviwi achaunza mutero; madzimambo eShebha neSebha vachaswededza zvipo.
\v	11	Hongu, madzimambo ose achakotamira pasi pamberi pake; marudzi ose achamushumira.
\v	12	Nokuti achanunura mushaiwi kana achidana; nemurombo kana asina mubatsiri.
\v	13	Achanzwira tsitsi murombo nemushaiwi, uye achaponesa mweya yevashaiwi.
\v	14	Achadzikinura mweya wavo pakumanikidzwa nepautsinye; uye ropa ravo richava rakakosha pameso ake.
\v	15	Zvino achararama, uye kwaari kuchapiwa zvegoridhe reShebha; nemunyengetero uchaitirwa iye nguva nenguva; acharumbidzwa zuva rose.
\v	16	Kuchava nekuwanda kwezviyo panyika panhongonya dzemakomo; zvibereko zvazvo zvichazuzika seRebhanoni; uye vachabuka kubva muguta seuswa hwenyika.
\v	17	Zita rake richavapo kusvika pakusingaperi, uye zita rake richawedzera kana zuva richingovapo. Uye vacharopafadzwa maari, marudzi ose achamuti: Wakaropafadzwa.
\p
\v	18	Ngaarumbidzwe Jehovha Mwari, Mwari waIsraeri, iye oga anoita zvishamiso.
\v	19	Ngarirumbidzwe zita rake rine rukudzo kusvika rinhi narinhi; nyika yose yakazara nerukudzo rwake, Ameni, uye Ameni.
\p
\v	20	Minyengetero yaDhavhidhi mwanakomana waJese yapera.
\c	73
\s	Kutambudzika kwevakaipa
\p
\v	1	ZvirokwazvoMwari wakanaka kuna Israeri, kune vakachena pamoyo.
\v	2	Asikana ndiri ini, tsoka dzangu dzakapotsa dzaenda, nhanho dzangu dzakapotsa dzatedzemuka.
\v	3	Nokutindaigodora vanozvikudza, ndaona kubudirira kwevakaipa.
\v	4	Nokutihapana zvisungo pakufa kwavo; uye muviri wavo wakakora.
\v	5	Havasimudambudziko remunhu; uye havatambudzwi nevanhu.
\v	6	Naizvozvokuzvikudza kunovakomberedza seruketani; kumanikidza kunovafukidza  senguvo.
\v	7	Mesoavo anobuda nekukora; mirangariro yemoyo inofashamira.
\v	8	Vanoseka,uye vanotaura zvakaipa nezvemanikidzo; vanotaura vari pakuzvikudza.
\v	9	Vanomisamuromo wavo kupikisa matenga; nerurimi rwavo rwunofamba panyika.
\v	10	Naizvozvo vanhu vake vanodzoka pano, uye mvura dzekuzara dzinosvinirwa ivo.
\v	11	Zvino vanoti: Mwari anoziva sei? Uye kune ruzivo here kune Wekumusoro-soro?
\v	12	Tarirai, ava ndevasina Mwari; zvakadaro vanobudirira panyika, vanowanza fuma.
\p
\v	13	Zvirokwazvo ndakanatsa moyo wangu pasina, nekushambidza maoko angu mukusava nemhosva.
\v	14	Nokuti zuva rose ndakatambudzwa, nekurangwa kwangu mangwanani oga-oga.
\v	15	Kana ndaiti: Ndichataura seizvi; tarirai, ndingadai ndakanyengera zera revanakomana venyu.
\v	16	Pandinorangarira kuziva izvi, zvinondirwadza pameso pangu.
\v	17	Kusvika ndapinda panzvimbo tsvene dzaMwari, ndakanzwisisa kuguma kwavo.
\v	18	Zvirokwazvo munovamisa panzvimbo dzinotedza; munovawisira mukuparadza kukuru.
\v	19	Haiwa, kuparara kwavo kwakaita sekubwaira kweziso! Vanopera vapedzwe nezvinotyisa.
\v	20	Sechiroto pakupepuka, Ishe, pamunomuka muchazvidza mufananidzo wavo.
\p
\v	21	Saizvozvo moyo wangu wakarwadziwa, uye ndakabaiwa paitsvo dzangu.
\v	22	Uye ndakava benzi risingazivi, ndakava mhuka kwamuri.
\v	23	Zvakadaro ndinemwi nguva nenguva; makabata ruoko rwangu rwerudyi.
\v	24	Muchanditungamirira nezano renyu, uye shure kweizvozvo munondigamuchira  mukubwinya.
\v	25	Ndinaani kudenga,  kunze kwenyu? Uye hakuna chandinoshuva panyika kunze kwenyu.
\v	26	Nyama yangu nemoyo wangu zvinopera; Mwari ndiye dombo remoyo wangu nemugove wangu kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	27	Nokuti tarirai, avo vari kure nemwi vachaparara; makaparadza vose vanopomba vachibva kwamuri.
\v	28	Asi ini, zvakandinakira kuswedera kuna Mwari; ndakaisa utiziro hwangu kuna Ishe Jehovha, kurondedzera zviito zvenyu zvose.
\c	74
\s	Kukumbira kuti Mwari abatsire vanhu vake
\p
\v	1	Mwari,sei maka tirasa nekusingaperi? Hasha dzenyu dzinopfungairi rei makwai emafuro enyu?
\v	2	Rangariraiungano yenyu  yamakatenga kare, tsvimbo yenhaka yenyu  yamakadzikinura; gomo iri reZiyoni makagara mariri.
\v	3	Simudziraitsoka dzenyu kukuparadza kukuru kunoenderera, zvose zvakaipa muvengi zvawakaita panzvimbo tsvene.
\p
\v	4	Vavengivenyu vakaomba pakati penzvimbo dzenyu dzekuungana; vakamisa zviratidzo zvavo kuva zviratidzo.
\v	5	Munhu anozikanwa seanosimudza masanhu musango remiti.
\v	6	Asiikozvino vanoputsa zvose zvakafomborwa zvayo nedimuro nedzinyundo.
\v	7	Vakapaimba yenyu tsvene kumoto; zvakasvibisa nzvimbo yekugara yezita renyu kusvika muvhu.
\v	8	Vakatimumoyo wavo: Ngativatsikirire pamwe chete; vakapisa nzvimbo dzose dzekuungana dzaMwari panyika.
\p
\v	9	Hationizviratidzo zvedu; hapachina muporofita; uye pakati pedu hapana anoziva  kuti kusvika rinhi.
\v	10	Mwari, kusvika rinhi mudzivisi achishora? Muvengi achazvidza zita renyu nekusingaperi here?
\v	11	Munodzoserei ruoko rwenyu, irwo ruoko rwenyu rwerudyi?  Rwubvisei kubva mukati mechipfuva chenyu.
\p
\v	12	Zvakadaro Mwari ndiMambo wangu kubva kare, anoita ruponeso rukuru pakati penyika.
\v	13	Ndimwi makapamura gungwa nesimba renyu; makaputsa misoro yemabukanana mumvura.
\v	14	Ndimwi makaputsanya misoro yeRevhiyatani; mukamupa kuva zvekudya zvevanhu murenje.
\v	15	Ndimwi makapamura zvitubu nerukova; ndimwi makaomesa nzizi dzenguva dzose.
\v	16	Zuva nderenyu, neusiku ndehwenyu; ndimwi makagadzira chiedza nezuva.
\v	17	Ndimwi makamisa miganhu yose yepanyika; zhizha nechando makazviumba.
\p
\v	18	Rangarirai ichi; muvengi wakazvidza Jehovha; uye rudzi benzi rwakanyomba zita renyu.
\v	19	Regai kupa mweya wenjiva yenyu kumhuka; musakanganwa chaunga chevatambudziki venyu nekusingaperi.
\v	20	Cherekedzai sungano; nokuti nzvimbo dzine rima dzepanyika dzizere neugaro hwemanikidzo.
\v	21	Anomanikidzwa ngaarege kudzoka achinyara; murombo nemushaiwi ngavarumbidze zita renyu.
\p
\v	22	Mukai, Mwari, mumiririre nyaya yenyu; murangarire kuzvidzwa kwenyu kubva kubenzi zuva rose.
\v	23	Regai kukanganwa inzwi revavengi venyu; ruzha rwevanokumukirai rwunokwira nguva nenguva.
\c	75
\s	Mwari ndiye mutongi
\p
\v	1	Tinopakuvonga kwamuri, Mwari; tinopa kuvonga kuti zita renyu riri pedo; vanorondedzera mabasa enyu anoshamisa.
\v	2	Kanandichigamuchira nguva yakatarwa, ini ndichatonga zvakarurama.
\v	3	Nyikanevagari vayo vose zvanyauka; ini ndakasimbisa mbiru dzayo. Sera.
\p
\v	4	Ndakatikune vanozvikudza: Musava vanozvikudza. Nekune vakaipa: Regai kusimudza runyanga.
\v	5	Regaikusimudza runyanga rwenyu kumusoro,  uye kutaura nemutsipa mukukutu.
\v	6	Nokutikukudzwa hakubvi kumabvazuva, kana kumavirira, uye hakubvi kurenje.
\v	7	AsiMwari mutongi; anoninipisa umwe uye achikudza umwe.
\v	8	Nokutimuruoko rwaJehovha mune mukombe; newaini inopupuma; uzere nemusanganiswa; uye anodurura kubva mauri; asi masese awo, vakaipa vose vepanyika vachaasvina vanwe.
\p
\v	9	Asiini ndichaparidza nekusingaperi; ndiimbire Mwari waJakove rumbidzo.
\v	10	Nenyanga dzose dzevakaipa ndichagura; nyanga dzevakarurama dzichasimudzwa.
\c	76
\s	Mwari mukundi uye mutongi
\p
\v	1	Mwarianozikanwa kwaJudha; zita rake iguru kwaIsraeri.
\v	2	PaSaremiwopane dumbu rake, nenzvimbo yake yekugara paZiyoni.
\v	3	Ipapoanovhuna miseve inopfuta yeuta, nhovo, nemunondo, nehondo. Sera.
\v	4	Munobwinya,munoremekedzwa kupfuura makomo ezvakapambiwa.
\v	5	Vakapambwavakasimba pamoyo; vakarara hope dzavo; uye hakuna pamhare vakawana maoko avo.
\v	6	Pakutsiurakwenyu, Mwari waJakove, zvose ngoro nebhiza zvinorara hope huru.
\v	7	Imwi,iyemwi munotyisa; uye ndiani angamira pamberi penyu kubva panguva yekutsamwa kwenyu?
\v	8	Makanzwisamutongo kubva kudenga; nyika yakatya ndokunyarara,
\v	9	Mwaripaanomukira mutongo, kuponesa vose vanyoro venyika. Sera.
\v	10	Zvirokwazvo, kutsamwa kwemunhu kuchakurumbidzai; muchasunga chiuno nemusiiwa wekutsamwa kukuru.
\v	11	Pikai, muripire Jehovha Mwari wenyu; vose vakamupoteredza ngavauye nezvipo kuna iye anofanira kutyiwa.
\v	12	Achagura mweya wemachinda; anotyisa kumadzimambo enyika.
\c	77
\s	Kusimbiswa kunobva pakurangarira mabasa ekare aMwari
\p
\v	1	Inzwirangu riri kuna Mwari, uye ndinochema; inzwi rangu riri kuna Mwari, iye ndokupa nzeve kwandiri.
\v	2	Pazuvarekutambudzika kwangu ndakatsvaka Ishe. Ruoko rwangu rwaiva rwakatandavadzwa usiku, uye harwuna kuneta; mweya wangu wakaramba kunyaradzwa.
\v	3	NdinorangariraMwari, uye ndakavovora; ndinofungisisa, uye mweya weupenyu wangu wakaziya. Sera.
\p
\v	4	Makabatameso angu kuti asarara; ndakatambudzika, uye handina kutaura.
\v	5	Ndakarangariramazuva ekare, makore ekare-kare.
\v	6	Ndinozviyeudzirakuimba kwangu pausiku; ndinotaurirana nemoyo wangu; nemweya weupenyu wangu wakanzvera.
\p
\v	7	Isheangarasa zvachose here? Uye haangavizve netsitsi zvekare here?
\v	8	Rudorweunyoro hwake rwaguma nekusingaperi here? Chivimbiso chapera kubva kuzera kusvika kuzera here?
\v	9	Mwariwakanganwa kuva nenyasha here? Wakapfigira tsitsi dzake nekutsamwa here? Sera.
\p
\v	10	Zvino ndakati: Uhwu utera hwangu, makore eruoko rwerudyi rweWekumusoro-soro.
\v	11	Ndicharangarira mabasa aJehovha; zvirokwazvo, ndicharangarira zvishamiso zvenyu zvekare.
\v	12	Ndichafungisisawo zvebasa renyu rose, uye ndinotaura zvezviito zvenyu.
\v	13	Mwari, nzira yenyu iri panzvimbo tsvene. Ndiani mwari mukuru saMwari?
\v	14	Imwi muri Mwari anoita chishamiso; makazivisa simba renyu pakati pemarudzi.
\v	15	Makadzikinura vanhu venyu neruoko  rwenyu, vanakomana vaJakove naJosefa. Sera.
\p
\v	16	Mvura zhinji yakakuonai, Mwari; mvura zhinji yakakuonai; yakatya; udziku ukuruwo hwakadedera.
\v	17	Makore akadurura mvura; matenga akabudisa ruzha; miseve yenyuwo yakaenda uko neuko.
\v	18	Inzwi remutinhiro wenyu riri muchamupupuri; mheni dzakavheneka nyika; pasi pakabvunda nekuzununguka.
\v	19	Nzira yenyu iri mugungwa, negwara renyu riri mumvura zhinji zhinji, nenhanho dzenyu dzaiva dzisingazikanwi.
\v	20	Makatungamirira vanhu venyu seboka remakwai neruoko rwaMozisi naAroni.
\c	78
\s	Rangarirai zvamakaitirwa
\p
\v	1	Ipainzeve, vanhu vangu,  kumurau wangu; rerekerai nzeve yenyu kumashoko emuromo wangu.
\v	2	Ndichashamisamuromo wangu nemufananidzo; ndichabudisa zvakavanzika zvekare,
\v	3	zvatakanzwanezvatinoziva, uye madzibaba edu akatirondedzera.
\v	4	Hatingavanzirivana vavo, kuzera rinotevera, tichirondedzera rumbidzo dzaJehovha, nesimba rake, nezvishamiso zvake, zvaakaita.
\p
\v	5	Nokutiwakamisa chipupuro kwaJakove, ndokutema murau kwaIsraeri, waakaraira madzibaba edu, kuti vazivise vana vavo.
\v	6	Kutizera rinotevera rizive, vana vachazvarwa, vasimuke ndokurondedzera vana vavo.
\v	7	Kutivaise tariro yavo kuna Mwari, uye vasakanganwa mabasa aMwari, asi vachengete mirau yake.
\v	8	Uyevasava semadzibaba avo, zera risingateereri uye rinopanduka, zera  risina kururamisa moyo waro, uye remweya waro usina kutendeka kuna Mwari.
\p
\v	9	VanavaEfuremu, vakashonga zvombo, vafuri veuta, vakadzokera shure nezuva rehondo.
\v	10	Havana kuchengeta sungano yaMwari, uye vakaramba kufamba mumurau wake.
\v	11	Zvino vakakanganwa zviito zvake nezvishamiso zvake zvaakavaratidza.
\p
\v	12	Wakaita chinhu chinoshamisa pamberi pemadzibaba avo, panyika yeEgipita, sango reZoani.
\v	13	Wakapamura gungwa, ndokuvayambusa; uye akamisa mvura zhinji semurwi.
\v	14	Masikatiwo wakavatungamirira negore, neusiku hwose nechiedza chemoto.
\v	15	Wakapamura mabwe murenje, akavanwisa kwazvo se zvinobva  paudziku ukuru.
\v	16	Wakabudisawo hova kubva padombo, ndokuburusisa mvura zhinji senzizi.
\p
\v	17	Asi vakaendererazve kumutadzira kusvika pakumukira Wekumusoro-soro murenje.
\v	18	Zvino vakaidza Mwari mumoyo wavo nekukumbira zvekudya zveruchiva rwavo.
\v	19	Zvino vakataura vachipikisa Mwari vachiti: Mwari angagona kugadzira tafura murenje here?
\v	20	Tarirai, wakarova dombo, mvura zhinji ndokuyerera, hongu, hova dzakapfachukira. Angagona kupawo chingwa here? Angagadzirira vanhu vake nyama here?
\v	21	Naizvozvo Jehovha wakanzwa, ndokutsamwa; uye moto wakapfutidzirwa Jakove, uye kutsamwawo kwakamukira Israeri.
\v	22	Nokuti havana kutenda Mwari, uye havana kuvimba neruponeso rwake.
\v	23	Kunyange akaraira makore kubva kumusoro, ndokuzarura magonhi ematenga.
\v	24	Zvino wakanaisa mana pamusoro pavo kuti vadye, wakavapa zviyo zvematenga.
\v	25	Munhu akadya chingwa chevane simba; wakavatumira zvekudya kuti  vagute.
\v	26	Wakavhuvhutisa mhepo yemabvazuva kumatenga, uye nesimba rake wakafambisa mhepo yechamhembe.
\v	27	Wakanaisawo nyama pamusoro pavo seguruva, neshiri dzine mapapiro sejecha regungwa.
\v	28	Waka zviwisira pakati pemusasa wavo, kupoteredza nzvimbo dzavo dzekugara.
\v	29	Zvino vakadya ndokuguta kwazvo, nokuti wakavavigira chishuvo chavo.
\v	30	Havana kuparadzaniswa nechishuvo chavo, zvekudya zvavo zvichiri mumuromo mavo,
\v	31	kutsamwa kwaMwari kwakavamukira, ndokuuraya pakati pevakakoresa vavo, ndokurova vasanangurwa kwaIsraeri.
\p
\v	32	Pane izvi zvose vakaramba vachitadza, uye havana kutenda nekuda kwezvishamiso zvake.
\v	33	Naizvozvo wakapedza mazuva avo nezvisina maturo, nemakore avo pakuvhunduka.
\v	34	Paakavauraya, vakamutsvaka, vakatendeuka, ndokutsvakisisa Mwari.
\v	35	Zvino vakarangarira kuti Mwari idombo ravo, naMwari Wekumusoro-soro mudzikunuri wavo.
\v	36	Asi vakamunyengedza nemuromo wavo, ndokumurevera nhema nerurimi rwavo.
\v	37	Nokuti moyo wavo waiva usina kururama kwaari, uye usina kutendeka pasungano yake.
\v	38	Asi iye, ari ane tsitsi, wakakanganwira uipi, uye haana kuparadza, hongu, nguva zhinji wakadzosa kutsamwa kwake, uye haana kumutsa kutsamwa kwake kose.
\v	39	Nokuti wakarangarira kuti vaiva nyama, mhepo inopfuura uye isingadzoki.
\p
\v	40	Kazhinji sei vachimumukira murenje, vakamushungurudza mugwenga!
\v	41	Hongu, vakadzoka vakaedza Mwari, vakashungurudza Mutsvene waIsraeri.
\v	42	Havana kurangarira ruoko rwake, zuva raakavadzikinura pamuvengi.
\v	43	Kuti wakamisa sei zviratidzo zvake paEgipita, nezvishamiso zvake pasango reZoani.
\v	44	Uye wakashandura nzizi dzavo kuva ropa, nehova dzavo, kuti vasanwa.
\v	45	Wakatuma pakati pavo mapupira enhunzi dzakavadya; nematacha akavaparadza.
\v	46	Zvibereko zvavo wakazvipawo kumhunduru, nebasa ravo kumhashu.
\v	47	Wakaparadza muzambiringa wavo nechimvuramabwe, nemionde yavo nechando chakachena.
\v	48	Wakapawo zvipfuwo zvavo kuchimvuramabwe, nemapoka avo kumheni.
\v	49	Wakatumira pakati pavo kutyisa kwehasha dzake, kutsamwa neshungu nekutambudzika,  nekutuma vatumwa vezvakaipa zvizhinji.
\v	50	Wakagadzirira hasha dzake nzira, haana kurega mweya wavo parufu, asi wakapa upenyu hwavo kuhosha.
\v	51	Zvino wakarova dangwe rose muEgipita, chekutanga chesimba pamatende aHami.
\v	52	Zvino wakabudisa vanhu vake semakwai, nekuvaperekedza murenje seboka.
\v	53	Zvino wakavatungamirira vakachengetedzeka kuti vasatya; asi gungwa rakafukidza vavengi vavo.
\v	54	Zvino wakavasvitsa pamuganhu wenzvimbo yake tsvene, gomo iri, ruoko rwake rwerudyi  zvarwakawana.
\v	55	Wakadzingawo vechirudzi pamberi pavo, ndokugovera pakati pavo nhaka nemutaro, ndokugarisa marudzi aIsraeri mumatende avo.
\p
\v	56	Zvakadaro vakaedza, uye vakamukira Mwari Wekumusoro-soro, uye havana kuchengeta zvipupuriro zvake.
\v	57	Asi vadzokera shure ndokuita nekusavimbika semadzibaba avo; vakatsauswa seuta hunonyengera.
\v	58	Nokuti vakamutsamwisa nenzvimbo dzavo dzakakwirira, nekumumutsira godo nezvifananidzo zvavo zvakavezwa.
\v	59	Mwari wakanzwa, wakatsamwa, ndokusema Israeri zvikuru,
\v	60	zvekuti wakasiya tabhenakeri yeShiro, tende raakamisa pakati pevanhu.
\v	61	Zvino wakapa simba rake kuutapwa, nekubwinya kwake kuruoko rwemuvengi.
\v	62	Nekupa vanhu vake kumunondo; uye wakatsamwira nhaka yake.
\v	63	Moto wakapedza majaya avo; uye mhandara dzavo hadzina kurumbidzwa.
\v	64	Vapristi vavo vakawa nemunondo; uye chirikadzi dzavo hadzina kuchema.
\p
\v	65	Ipapo Ishe wakamuka semurari, seane masimba anodanidzira nekuda kwewaini.
\v	66	Zvino wakarova vavengi vake necheshure; akavaisa chinyadzo nekusingaperi.
\v	67	Wakarambawo tende raJosefa, uye haana kusanangura rudzi rwaEfuremu.
\v	68	Asi wakasanangura rudzi rwaJudha, gomo reZiyoni raaida.
\v	69	Zvino wakavaka nzvimbo yake tsvene sedzinhongonya, senyika yaakateya kusvika rinhi.
\v	70	Wakasanangurawo Dhavhidhi muranda wake, ndokumutora kubva kumatanga emakwai.
\v	71	Kubva pakutevera matunzvi wakamuuisa kufudza Jakove vanhu vake, naIsraeri nhaka yake.
\v	72	Naizvozvo wakavafudza zvichienderana neuchokwadi hwemoyo wake, ndokuvatungamirira neunyanzvi hwemaoko ake.
\c	79
\s	Kukumbira Mwari kuti abatsire vanhu vake
\p
\v	1	Mwari,vahedheni vapinda panhaka yenyu; vakasvibisa tembere yenyu tsvene; Jerusarema vakariita rive mirwi.
\v	2	Zvitunhazvevaranda venyu vakapa shiri dzematenga kuva zvekudya, nyama yevatsvene venyu kuzvikara zvenyika.
\v	3	Vakateuraropa ravo semvura mativi ose paJerusarema; uye hapana kuva neanoviga.
\v	4	Tavachinyadzo kuvavakidzani vedu, chiseko nechizvidzwa kune vakatipoteredza.
\p
\v	5	Kusvikarinhi, Jehovha? Muchatsamwa nekusingaperi here? Godo renyu richapfuta semoto here?
\v	6	Dururaihasha dzenyu pamusoro pevahedheni vasingakuziviyi, nepamusoro peushe uzhinji husingadani zita renyu.
\v	7	Nokutivakadya Jakove, neugaro hwake vakahuita dongo.
\v	8	Musarangarirazvivi zvekare kutirwisa; tsitsi dzenyu ngadzikurumidze kuuya pamberi pedu, nokuti takaneta kwazvo.
\v	9	Tibatsirei,Mwari weruponeso rwedu, nekuda kwekukudzwa kwezita renyu; uye tinunurei nekuripira zvivi zvedu nekuda kwezita renyu.
\v	10	Sei vahedheni vachiti: Mwari wavo aripi? Ngaazikanwe pakati pevahedheni pamberi pemeso edu, tsivo yeropa revaranda venyu rakateurwa.
\p
\v	11	Kugomera kwemusungwa ngakuuye pamberi penyu; zvichienderana neukuru hweruoko renyu muchengetedze vana verufu.
\v	12	Uye mutsivire vavakidzani vedu kanomwe pachipfuva chavo, kushora kwavo kwavakakushorai nako, Ishe.
\v	13	Naizvozvo isu, vanhu venyu, nemakwai emafuro enyu, tichakuvongai nekusingaperi; ticharondedzera kurumbidzwa kwenyu kuzera nezera.
\c	8
\s	Kukudzwa kwemunhu naJehovha
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,Ishe wedu, rinobwinya sei zita renyu panyika yose! Imwi makaisa kubwinya kwenyu kumusoro kumatenga.
\p
\v	2	Pamiromoyevacheche nevanoyamwa makagadza simba nekuda kwevavengi venyu, kuti munyaradze muvengi nemutsivi.
\v	3	Kanandichicherekedza matenga enyu, basa reminwe yenyu, mwedzi nenyeredzi zvamakamisa:
\v	4	Munhuchii zvamunomurangarira? Nemwanakomana wemunhu zvamunomushanyira?
\v	5	Nokutimakamuita ave pasi zvishoma kuvatumwa, makamushongedza korona yeumambo nerukudzo.
\v	6	Makamuitaatonge pamusoro pemabasa emaoko enyu; zvose makaisa pasi petsoka dzake:
\v	7	Makwai,nenzombe zvose, uyewo mhuka dzesango,
\v	8	shiridzematenga, nehove dzegungwa, dzinopfuura panzira dzemakungwa.
\p
\v	9	Jehovha,Ishe wedu, rinobwinya sei zita renyu panyika yose!
\c	80
\s	Munyengetero wekubatsirwa kwaIsraeri
\p
\v	1	Ipainzeve, mufudzi waIsraeri, imwi munotungamirira Josefa seboka, mugere  pamakerubhi, penyai!
\v	2	Mutsaisimba renyu pamberi paEfuremu naBhenjamini naManase, muuye kuva ruponeso rwedu.
\p
\v	3	Tidzoserei,Mwari, uye penyesai chiso chenyu, zvino tichaponeswa.
\p
\v	4	Jehovha,Mwari wedzihondo, kusvika rinhi makatsamwira munyengetero wevanhu venyu?
\v	5	Makavadyisachingwa chemisodzi, nekuvanwisa misodzi nechiyero.
\v	6	Makatiitagakava kuvavakidzani vedu, uye vavengi vedu vanoseka pakati pavo.
\p
\v	7	Tidzoserei,Mwari wedzihondo, uye penyesai chiso chenyu, zvino tichaponeswa.
\p
\v	8	Makaunzamuzambiringa kubva muEgipita, makadzinga vahedheni, ndokuusima.
\v	9	Makagadzirirapamberi pawo, nekudzikisa midzi yawo, kusvika wazara nyika.
\v	10	Makomo akafukidzwa nemumvuri wawo, nematavi awo, misidhari yaMwari.
\v	11	Wakatandisira matavi awo kugungwa, nemabukira awo kusvika kurwizi.
\v	12	Makaputsirei masvingo awo, kuti vose vanopfuura nenzira vautanhe?
\v	13	Nguruve yesango inouparadza, nemhuka yesango inoufura.
\p
\v	14	Mwari wehondo, dzokai henyu, mutarise pasi muri kumatenga, zvino muone, mugocherekedza muzambiringa uyu.
\v	15	Uye mudzi ruoko rwako rwerudyi warwakasima, nedavi ramakazvisimbisira.
\v	16	Wapiswa nemoto, watemerwa pasi; vanoparara nekutsiura kwechiso chenyu.
\v	17	Ruoko rwenyu ngarwuve pamusoro pemunhu weruoko rwenyu rwerudyi, pamusoro pemwanakomana wemunhu,  wamakazvisimbisira.
\v	18	Naizvozvo hatingadzoki kubva kwamuri; tivandudzei, ipapo tichadana nezita renyu.
\p
\v	19	Jehovha, Mwari wehondo; tidzorei, penyesai chiso chenyu, zvino tichaponeswa.
\c	81
\s	Kusateerera kwaIsraeri
\p
\v	1	Imbiraikwazvo Mwari, simba redu; pururudzirai Mwari waJakove.
\v	2	Torairwiyo, mugounza gandira, mbira inonakidza pamwe nemutengeranwa.
\v	3	Ridzaihwamanda pakugara kwemwedzi, panguva yakatarwa, pazuva remutambo wedu.
\v	4	Nokutiichi chimiso chaIsraeri, murau waMwari waJakove.
\v	5	Wakazvitemakuva chipupuro muna Josefa, pakubuda kwake kurwisa nyika yeEgipita; ndakanzwa rurimi rwandaiva ndisingazivi.
\p
\v	6	Ndakabvisafudzi rake kubva pamutoro; maoko ake akapfuudzwa kubva muhari.
\v	7	Wakadanauri mudambudziko, zvino ndakakununura; ndakakupindura panzvimbo yakavanda yemutinhiro; ndakakunzvera pamvura zhinji dzeMeribha. Sera.
\v	8	Inzwai,vanhu vangu, zvino ndichakupupurirai; Israeri, dai waindinzwa!
\v	9	Hapangavinamwari wevatorwa pakati pako, uye usingakotamiri mwari wekumwe.
\v	10	Ndiri Jehovha Mwari wako, wakakukwidza kubva panyika yeEgipita; shamisa muromo wako kwazvo, zvino ndichauzadza.
\p
\v	11	Asi vanhu vangu havana kuteerera kuinzwi rangu; uye Israeri haana kutenderana neni.
\v	12	Naizvozvo ndakavapa mukusindimara kwemoyo wavo,  kuti vafambe mumazano avo.
\p
\v	13	Haiwa, dai vanhu vangu vainditeerera, Israeri aifamba munzira dzangu!
\v	14	Nekukurumidza ndingadai ndaderedza vavengi vavo, nekushandukirira ruoko rwangu kuvadzivisi vavo.
\v	15	Vanovenga Jehovha vanozviisa pasi pake nekunyepedzera; asi nguva yavo yaivapo nekusingaperi.
\v	16	Waizovadyisawo gorosi rakaisvonaka; uye ndaikugutsa neuchi hunobva padombo.
\c	82
\s	Mwari ndiye mutongi mukuru
\p
\v	1	Mwarianomira paungano yemasimba; anotonga pakati pevamwari.
\p
\v	2	Kusvikarinhi muchitonga zvisina kururama, uye muchigamuchira chiso chevakaipa? Sera.
\v	3	Tongeraivarombo nenherera; ruramisirai vanotambudzika nevanoshaiwa.
\v	4	Pukunyutsaimurombo nemushaiwi, nunurai kubva muruoko rwevakaipa.
\v	5	Havazivi,havanzwisisi; vanofamba-famba murima; nheyo dzose dzenyika dzinozununguka.
\v	6	Inindakati: Muri vamwari, uye mose muri vanakomana veWekumusoro-soro.
\v	7	Asimuchafa semunhu, nekuwa seumwe wemachinda.
\p
\v	8	Mukai,Mwari, mutonge nyika; nokuti imwi, ndudzi dzose inhaka yenyu.
\c	83
\s	Munyengetero wekuti vavengi vaIsraeri vaparadzwe
\p
\v	1	Mwari,regai kunyarara; regai kusataura, uye musati zii, Mwari.
\v	2	Nokutitarirai, vavengi venyu vanoita bope; uye vanokuvengai vakasimudza musoro.
\p
\v	3	Vanotoreravanhu venyu zano reunyengeri, vanorangana pamusoro pevakavanzwa venyu.
\v	4	Vakati:Uyai, ngativaparadzei kubva pakuva rudzi, kuti zita raIsraeri risava richarangarirwazve.
\v	5	Nokutivakarangana  nemoyo umwe; vanoita sungano kurwisana nemwi.
\v	6	MatendeaEdhomu, nevaIshimaeri, Moabhu, nevaHagari,
\v	7	Gebhari,naAmoni, naAmareki, Firisitia, pamwe nevagari veTire,
\v	8	Ashuriwowakazvibatanidza navo; vaiva ruoko pavana vaRoti. Sera.
\p
\v	9	MuvaitiresaMidhiani, saSisera, saJabhini, parukova Kishoni.
\v	10	Vakaparadzwa paEndori; vakava mupfudze wevhu.
\v	11	Itai vakuru vavo saOrebhi uye saZeebhi; hongu, machinda avo ose saZebha uye saZarimuna.
\v	12	Ivo vakati: Ngatizvitorere mafuro aMwari ave edu.
\v	13	Mwari wangu, muvaite sechinyamupupuri, semakoto pamberi pemhepo.
\v	14	Semoto unopisa sango, uye semurazvo unotungidza makomo.
\v	15	Naizvozvo muvadzingirire nedutu renyu remhepo, uye muvatyityidzire nechamupupuri chenyu.
\v	16	Zadzai zviso zvavo nenyadzi, kuti vatsvake zita renyu, Jehovha.
\v	17	Ngavanyadziswe uye vavhunduswe nekusingaperi; zvirokwazvo, ngavasvodeswe uye vaparare.
\v	18	Kuti vazive kuti ndimwi moga,  mune zita renyu ndiJehovha, Wekumusoro-soro pamusoro penyika yose.
\c	84
\s	Mufaro uri paimba yaMwari
\p
\v	1	Dzinodikasei tabhenakeri dzenyu, Jehovha wehondo!
\p
\v	2	Mweyaweupenyu wangu unoshuva, zvirokwazvo unopanga vazhe dzaJehovha; moyo wangu nenyama yangu zvinodana kuna Mwari mupenyu.
\v	3	Zvirokwazvodhimba yakawana imba, nenyenganyenga dendere rayo, painoisa vana vayo, aritari dzenyu, Jehovha wehondo, Mambo wangu, naMwari wangu.
\v	4	Vakaropafadzwavanogara mumba menyu; vachagara vachikurumbidzai. Sera.
\v	5	Wakaropafadzwamunhu uyo simba rake riri mamuri, mune nzira huru mumoyo mavo.
\v	6	Avovanopfuura nemumupata weBhaka vanouita tsime; hongu, nemaropafadzo mvura yenhuruka inoputira.
\v	7	Vanofambakubva pasimba kuenda pasimba;  umwe neumwe aonekwe pamberi paMwari paZiyoni.
\p
\v	8	Jehovha,Mwari wedzihondo, inzwa munyengetero wangu; ipai nzeve, Mwari waJakove. Sera.
\v	9	Tarirai,Mwari, nhovo yedu, mugotarisa chiso chemuzodzwa wenyu.
\v	10	Nokuti zuva pavazhe dzenyu riri nani pane churu. Ndinosarudza kuva pakurinda mukova muimba yaMwari wangu pane kugara mumatende euipi.
\v	11	Nokuti Jehovha Mwari izuva nenhovo; Jehovha achapa nyasha nerukudzo; haanganyimi zvakanaka kune vanofamba nekururama.
\p
\v	12	Jehovha wehondo, wakaropafadzwa munhu anovimba nemwi.
\c	85
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbirira Israeri rugare
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,makaitira nyasha nyika yenyu; makadzosa utapwa hwaJakove.
\v	2	Makakanganwirauipi hwevanhu venyu; makafukidza zvivi zvavo zvose. Sera.
\v	3	Makabvisakutsamwa kwenyu kose; makadzoka pakupfuta kwehasha dzenyu.
\v	4	Tidzosei,Mwari weruponeso rwedu; mugogumisa hasha dzenyu kwatiri.
\v	5	Muchatitsamwiranekusingaperi here? Mucharebesa hasha dzenyu kuzera nezera here?
\v	6	Imwihamungatimutsirudzizve here, kuti vanhu venyu vafare mamuri?
\v	7	Tiratidzeitsitsi dzenyu, Jehovha; mugotipa ruponeso rwenyu.
\p
\v	8	NdichanzwaMwari Jehovha zvaachataura; nokuti achataura rugare kuvanhu vake nekuvatsvene vake; asi ngavasadzokerazve kuupenzi.
\v	9	Zvirokwazvoruponeso rwake rwuri pedo kune vanomutya, kuti rukudzo rwugare panyika yekwedu.
\v	10	Tsitsi nechokwadi zvinochingamidzana; kururama nerugare zvakatsvod ana.
\v	11	Chokwadi chichamera kubva pasi; uye kururama kuchatarisa pasi kuri kumatenga.
\v	12	Zvirokwazvo Jehovha uchapa zvakanaka; uye nyika yedu ichapa zvibereko zvayo.
\v	13	Kururama kuchafamba pamberi pake, kugoitira nhanho dzake nzira.
\c	86
\s	Munyengetero wekukumbira tsitsi dzaMwari
\p
\v	1	Rerekainzeve yenyu, Jehovha, ndipindurei; nokuti ndiri murombo nemushaiwi.
\v	2	Chengetedzaimweya weupenyu wangu; nokuti ndiri wakatendeka; imwi Mwari wangu, ponesai muranda wenyu anovimba nemwi.
\v	3	Ndinzwireitsitsi, Ishe, nokuti ndinodana kwamuri zuva rose.
\v	4	Fadzaimweya weupenyu wemuranda wenyu, nokuti ndinosimudzira mweya weupenyu wangu kwamuri, Ishe.
\v	5	Nokutiimwi Ishe, makanaka, uye munokanganwira, uye muri mukuru patsitsi kune avo vose vanodana kwamuri.
\v	6	Ipainzeve, Jehovha, kumunyengetero wangu; uye muteerere kuinzwi remikumbiro yangu.
\v	7	Pazuvarekutambudzika kwangu ndichadana kwamuri, nokuti muchandipindura.
\p
\v	8	Hapanawakafanana nemwi pakati pevamwari, Ishe, uye hapana akaita semabasa enyu.
\v	9	Marudziose amakaita achauya akotama pamberi penyu, Ishe, arumbidze zita renyu.
\v	10	Nokuti muri mukuru, uye munoita zvinhu zvinoshamisa; muri Mwari moga.
\p
\v	11	Ndidzidzisei nzira yenyu, Jehovha; ndichafamba muchokwadi chenyu; batanidzai moyo wangu kuti utye zita renyu.
\v	12	Ndichakurumbidzai, Ishe Mwari wangu, nemoyo wangu wose, uye ndicharumbidza zita renyu nekusingaperi.
\v	13	Nokuti tsitsi dzenyu ihuru kwandiri; uye makanunura mweya weupenyu wangu kubva mugomba repasi-pasi.
\v	14	Mwari, vanozvikudza vakandimukira; uye ungano yevanomanikidza vanotsvaka mweya weupenyu wangu; uye havana kukuisai pamberi pavo.
\v	15	Asi imwi, Ishe, muri Mwari ane tsitsi nengoni, munononoka kutsamwa, uye muri mukuru patsitsi nechokwadi.
\v	16	Tendeukirai kwandiri, mugondinzwira tsitsi, ipai simba renyu kumuranda wenyu, uye ponesai mwanakomana wemurandakadzi wenyu.
\v	17	Ndiratidzei chiratidzo chezvakanaka, kuti vanondivenga vaone, uye vanyare, nokuti imwi Jehovha, makandibatsira nekundinyaradza.
\c	87
\s	Mbiri yeJerusarema
\p
\v	1	Nheyoyake iri pamusoro pemakomo matsvene.
\v	2	Jehovhaanoda masuwo eZiyoni kupfuura nzvimbo dzose dzekugara dzaJakove.
\v	3	Zvinhuzvinorumbidzwa zvinotaurwa pamusoro pako, guta raMwari! Sera.
\p
\v	4	NdichatauraRahabhi neBhabhironi kune vanondiziva; tarirai, Firisitia, neTire, pamwe neItiyopiya, uyu wakazvarirwako.
\v	5	Zvinopamusoro peZiyoni zvichanzi: Murume uyu neuyo vakazvarirwa mariri; uye Wekumusoro-soro amene acharisimbisa.
\v	6	Jehovhaachaverenga pakunyora kwake vanhu: Uyu wakazvarirwako. Sera.
\v	7	Vaimbipamwe nevatambi, matsime angu ose ari mauri.
\c	88
\s	Kuchema kwemunhu anotambudzika
\p
\v	1	Jehovha,Mwari weruponeso rwangu, ndakachema masikati neusiku pamberi penyu.
\v	2	Munyengeterowangu ngauuye pamberi penyu; rerekerai nzeve yenyu kukuchema kwangu.
\p
\v	3	Nokutimweya weupenyu wangu uzere nematambudziko, neupenyu hwangu hwonanavira kuguva.
\v	4	Ndinoverengwapamwe nevanoburukira kugomba; ndakaita semurume asina simba.
\v	5	Ndakasunungurwa pakati pevakafa, sevakaurawa varere muguva, vamusati mucharangarira; nokuti ivo vakagurwa vakabviswa paruoko rwenyu.
\v	6	Makandiisamugomba repasi-pasi, panzvimbo dzine rima, muudziku ukuru.
\v	7	Hashadzenyu dzinorema pamusoro pangu; makarwadzisa nemafungu enyu ose. Sera.
\v	8	Makabvisiravazikanwi vangu kure neni; makandiita chinyangadzo chikuru kwavari; ndavharirwa, uye handi goni kubuda.
\v	9	Zisorangu ropera nekuda kwekurwadziwa; Jehovha, ndakadana kwamuri nezuva rose; ndakatandavadzira maoko angu kwamuri.
\p
\v	10	Vakafa mungavaitira chishamiso here? Mweya yakafa ichamuka here ikakurumbidzai? Sera.
\v	11	Rudo rweunyoro hwenyu rwungarondedzerwa muguva here?  Nekutendeka kwenyu mukuparadza here?
\v	12	Zvishamiso zvenyu zvingazikanwa murima here? Nekururama kwenyu panyika yekukanganwa here?
\p
\v	13	Asi ini, Jehovha, ndakachema kwamuri; uye mangwanani munyengetero wangu uchauya pamberi penyu.
\p
\v	14	Jehovha, munorasirei mweya weupenyu wangu? Munovanzire i chiso chenyu kwandiri?
\v	15	Ndatambudzika uye ndiri anofa kubva paudiki; ndakatakura kutyisa kwenyu; ndinopererwa.
\v	16	Hasha dzenyu dzinopisa dzakapfuura pamusoro pangu; kutyisa kukuru kwenyu kwakandipedza.
\v	17	Zvakandikomberedza semvura zuva rose; zvakandipoteredza pamwe chete.
\v	18	Mudiwa neshamwari makaisa kure neni; vazikanwi vangu vari  murima.
\c	89
\s	Zvivimbiso zvaJehovha
\p
\v	1	Ndichaimbiratsitsi dzaJehovha nekusingaperi; nemuromo wangu ndichazivisa kutendeka kwenyu kuzera nezera.
\v	2	Nokutindakati: Tsitsi dzichavakwa nekusingaperi; muchasimbisa kutendeka kwenyu mumatenga momene.
\p
\v	3	Ndakaitasungano nemusanangurwa wangu; ndakapika kumuranda wangu Dhavhidhi:
\v	4	Ndichasimbisambeu yako kusvika rinhi narinhi, uye ndichavaka chigaro chako cheushe kusvika kuzera nezera. Sera.
\p
\v	5	Zvinomatenga acharumbidza zvishamiso zvenyu, Jehovha; nekutendeka kwenyu paungano yevatsvene.
\v	6	Nokutindiani muchadenga angaenzaniswa naJehovha?  Ndiani akaita saJehovha pakati pevanakomana vevane simba?
\v	7	Mwarianotyisa zvikuru paungano yevatsvene, uye anofanira kuremekedzwa pamusoro pevose vakamukomberedza.
\v	8	Jehovha,Mwari wehondo, ndiani ane simba semwi, Jehovha? Uye kutendeka kwenyu kwakakukomberedzai.
\v	9	Ndimwimutongi pamusoro pekuzvikudza kwegungwa; panomuka mafungu aro, imwi munoanyaradza.
\v	10	Imwi makaputsanya Rahabhi seuyo anourawa; makaparadzira vavengi venyu neruoko rwenyu rwune simba.
\v	11	Matenga ndeenyu, nepasi ndepenyuwo; nyika nekuzara kwayo, imwi makazviteya.
\v	12	Maodzanyemba nechamhembe, imwi makazvisika; Tabhori neHerimoni zvichafara muzita renyu.
\v	13	Mune chanza chine simba; ruoko renyu rwakasimba; ruoko rwenyu rwerudyi rwakakwirira.
\v	14	Kururama nemutongo inheyo yechigaro chenyu cheushe; tsitsi nechokwadi zvichafamba pamberi pechiso chenyu.
\p
\v	15	Vakaropafadzwa vanhu vanoziva mhururu; vachafamba muchiedza chechiso chenyu, Jehovha.
\v	16	Muzita renyu vachafara zuva rose; uye mukururama kwenyu vanokwiridzirwa.
\v	17	Nokuti imwi muri kubwinya kwesimba ravo; uye munyasha dzenyu runyanga rwedu ruchakwiridzirwa.
\v	18	Nokuti nhovo yedu ndeyaJehovha; namambo wedu ndeweMutsvene waIsraeri.
\p
\v	19	Ipapo makataura muchiratidzo kumutsvene wenyu ndokuti: Ndakaisa rubatsiro pamusoro pewemasimba; ndakakwiridzira musanangurwa muvanhu.
\v	20	Ndakawana Dhavhidhi muranda wangu; nemafuta angu matsvene ndamuzodza.
\v	21	Naye ruoko rwangu rwuchasimbiswa; chanza changuwo chichamusimbisa.
\v	22	Muvengi haangamumanikidzi; nemwanakomana wekuipa haangamutambudzi.
\v	23	Zvino ndichapwanya vavengi vake pamberi pechiso chake; uye ndicharova vanomuvenga.
\v	24	Asi kutendeka kwangu netsitsi dzangu zvichava naye; uye muzita rangu runyanga rwake rwuchakwiridzirwa.
\v	25	Zvino ndichaisa ruoko rwake mugungwa, neruoko rwake rwerudyi panzizi.
\v	26	Iye achadana kwandiri  achiti: Imwi muri baba vangu, Mwari wangu, nedombo reruponeso rwangu.
\v	27	Ndichamugadzawo kuva dangwe, wakakwiririsa pamadzimambo enyika.
\v	28	Ndichamuchengetera tsitsi dzangu nekusingaperi, nesungano yangu ichasimba kwaari.
\v	29	Zvino ndichamisa mbeu yake kusvika rinhi narinhi, nechigaro chake cheushe semazuva ematenga.
\p
\v	30	Kana vana vake vakasiya murau wangu, uye vakasafamba mumitongo yangu,
\v	31	kana vakasvibisa zvimiso zvangu, uye vakasachengeta mirau yangu,
\v	32	ipapo ndichashanyira chitadzo chavo netsvimbo, nekuipa kwavo neshamhu zhinji.
\v	33	Zvakadaro handingatongobvisi rudo rweunyoro hwangu kwaari, uye handinganyengeri mukutendeka kwangu.
\v	34	Sungano yangu handingaguri, uye handishanduri chakabuda pamiromo yangu.
\v	35	Ndakapika kamwe chete neutsvene hwangu: Handingarevi nhema kuna Dhavhidhi.
\v	36	Mbeu yake ichavapo kusvika rinhi narinhi, nechigaro chake cheushe sezuva pamberi pangu.
\v	37	Chichasimbiswa semwedzi kusvika rinhi narinhi, uye uchapupu huri muchadenga hwakasimba. Sera.
\p
\v	38	Asi imwi makarasa nekuramba; makatsamwira muzodzwa wenyu.
\v	39	Makashaisa maturo sungano yemuranda wenyu; makasvibisa korona yake panyika.
\v	40	Makaputsa masvingo ake ose; makaita nhare dzake dongo.
\v	41	Vanopamba vose vanopfuura nenzira; ndiye chiseko kuvavakidzani vake.
\v	42	Makakwiridzira ruoko rwerudyi rwevadzivisi vake; makafadza vavengi vake vose.
\v	43	Munodzosawo kwakapinza kwemunondo wake; uye hamuna kumumisa pahondo.
\v	44	Makagumisa kubwinya kwake, nekukanda chigaro chake cheushe pavhu.
\v	45	Makapfupisa mazuva eudiki hwake; makamufukidza nenyadzi. Sera.
\p
\v	46	Jehovha, kusvika rinhi, muchizvivanza nekusingaperi? Kutsamwa kwenyu kuchapfuta semoto here?
\v	47	Rangarira kuti nguva yeupenyu hwangu yakadii. Makasikirei vana vevanhu vose pasina?
\v	48	Ndiani munhu anorarama asingaoni rufu? Anganunura mweya weupenyu wake kubva muruoko rweguva here? Sera.
\v	49	Rudo rweunyoro hwenyu hwekutanga huripi, Ishe,  hwamakapika kuna Dhavhidhi nekutendeka kwenyu?
\v	50	Rangarirai, Ishe, chiseko chevaranda venyu; ndakatakura pachipfuva changu  zvishooro zvemarudzi ose mazhinji,
\v	51	vavengi venyu zvavakashoora nazvo, Jehovha, zvaakashoora nazvo makwara emuzodzwa wenyu.
\p
\v	52	Jehovha ngaavongwe kusvika rinhi narinhi. Ameni, uye Ameni.
\c	9
\s	Dhavhidhi anovonga kurwirwa naJehovha
\p
\v	1	NdichavongaJehovha nemoyo wangu wose; ndicharondedzera zvishamiso zvenyu zvose.
\v	2	Ndichafaranekupembera mamuri; ndichaimbira zita renyu rumbidzo, imwi Wekumusoro-soro.
\p
\v	3	Panodzokeravavengi vangu shure, vachawa, ndokuparara pamberi penyu.
\v	4	Nokutimakaita kodzero yangu nenyaya yangu; makagara pachigaro cheushe, makatonga zvakarurama.
\v	5	Makatsiuravahedheni; makaparadza wakaipa; zita ravo makadzima kusvika pakusingaperi narinhi.
\v	6	Vavengivakapera, kuparara kwava rinhi narinhi, uye makaparadza maguta; kurangarirwa kwavo kwaparara  pamwe navo.
\p
\v	7	AsiJehovha achagara kusvika pakusingaperi; chigaro chenyu cheushe wakachigadzirira mutongo.
\v	8	Zvinoiye achatonga nyika mukururama, anotonga vanhu muzvakarurama.
\v	9	UyeJehovha achava nhare yeanomanikidzwa, nhare panguva dzekutambudzika.
\v	10	Zvino vanoziva zita renyu vachavimba nemwi; nokuti imwi Jehovha hamuna kusiya vanokutsvakai.
\p
\v	11	Imbirai Jehovha rumbidzo, iye agere paZiyoni; dudzirai zviito zvake pakati pendudzi.
\v	12	Kana achitsvaka ropa, anovarangarira; haakanganwi kuchema kwevanotambudzika.
\v	13	Ndinzwirei tsitsi, Jehovha; onai dambudziko rangu pane vanondivenga, imwi munondisimudza kubva pamasuwo erufu;
\v	14	kuti ndirondedzere rumbidzo yenyu yose pamasuwo emukunda weZiyoni; ndichafara paruponeso rwenyu.
\v	15	Vahedheni vakanyura mugomba ravakaita; rutsoka rwavo rwakabatwa mumumbure wavakavanza.
\v	16	Jehovha wakazvizivisa; wakaita mutongo; wakaipa wakateyiwa pabasa remaoko ake. Higayoni. Sera.
\v	17	Vakaipa vachadzokera kugehena, marudzi ose anokanganwa Mwari.
\v	18	Nokuti mushaiwi haangakanganikwi rinhi narinhi, tariro yevarombo  haiparar i nekusingaperi.
\p
\v	19	Simukai Jehovha; munhu ngaarege kukunda; vahedheni ngavatongwe pamberi penyu.
\v	20	Vavhundutsei, Jehovha; vahedheni ngavazive kuti vanongova vanhu. Sera.
\c	90
\s	Kupfupika kweupenyu hwemunhu
\p
\v	1	Ishe,imwi maiva ugaro hwedu pazera nezera.
\v	2	Makomoasati azvarwa, kana mabereka pasi nenyika, iko kubva pakusingaperi kusvika pakusingaperi, imwi muri Mwari.
\p
\v	3	Munodzoseramunhu mukukuyiwa; ndokuti: Dzokai imwi vana vevanhu.
\v	4	Nokutimakore churu pameso enyu akaita sezuva razuro kana rapfuura, hongu, murindiro pausiku.
\v	5	Munovakukura;vava  sehope; mangwanani vakaita seuswa hunotunga.
\v	6	Mangwananihunopenya, nekutunga; madekwani hunochekwa ndokusvava.
\p
\v	7	Nokutitinopedzwa mukutsamwa kwenyu; uye nehasha dzenyu tinokanganiswa.
\v	8	Makaisazvitadzo zvedu pamberi penyu, zvakavanzika zvedu pachiedza chechiso chenyu.
\v	9	Nokutimazuva edu ose anopfuura mukutsamwa kwenyu; tinopedza makore edu sekutura befu.
\v	10	Mazuva emakore edu, maari  mune makore makumi manomwe, uye kana nekuda kwesimba makore makumi masere; zvakadaro kuzvikudza kwawo kutambudzika nenhamo; nokuti anokurumidza kugurwa, uye tinobhururuka ndokunyangarika.
\v	11	Ndiani anoziva simba rekutsamwa kwenyu; uye zvichienderana nekutyisa kwenyu,  dzakadaro hasha dzenyu.
\v	12	Naizvozvo tidzidzisei kuverenga mazuva edu, kuti tiwane moyo weuchenjeri.
\p
\v	13	Dzokai, Jehovha! Kusvika rinhi? Uye nzwirai tsitsi varanda venyu.
\v	14	Tigutsei mangwanani netsitsi dzenyu, kuti tifare, tifarisise nemazuva edu ose.
\v	15	Tifadzei zvinoenderana nemazuva amakatitambudza, makore atakaona zvakaipa.
\v	16	Basa renyu ngarionekwe kuvaranda venyu, nekubwinya kwenyu kuvana vavo.
\v	17	Uye kunaka kwaIshe Mwari wedu ngakuve pamusoro pedu; uye simbisai basa remaoko edu kwatiri; hongu, basa remaoko edu murisimbise.
\c	91
\s	Mufaro wemunhu anochengetwa naJehovha
\p
\v	1	Uyoagere panzvimbo yakavanda yeWekumusoro-soro achagara pamumvuri weWemasimbaose.
\p
\v	2	Ndichatipamusoro paJehovha:  Ndiye utiziro hwangu nenhare yangu, Mwari wangu, ndinovimba naye.
\v	3	Nokutiiye achakununura kubva parudzingi rwemuteyi, kubva pahosha yekuparadza kukuru.
\v	4	Achakufukidzaneminhenga yake, uye uchavimba pasi pemapapiro ake; chokwadi chake inhovo huru nenhovo diki.
\v	5	Haungatyichinotyisa pausiku, museve unobhururuka masikati,
\v	6	hoshainofamba murima, kuparadza kunoputsa masikati machena.
\v	7	Kurutivirwako kuchawa churu, negumi rezvuru paruoko rwako rwerudyi; hazvingaswederi kwauri.
\p
\v	8	Kogaunotarisa nemeso ako; ndokuona kutsiviwa kwevakaipa.
\v	9	Nokutiimwi Jehovha muri utiziro hwangu! Wakaita Wekumusoro-soro ave nzvimbo yako yekugara.
\v	10	Hapana chakaipa chingakuwira, uye dambudziko ripi neripi haringaswederi patende rako.
\v	11	Nokuti acharaira vatumwa vake pamusoro pako, kukuchengetedza panzira dzako dzose.
\v	12	Vachakusimudza pamaoko, zvimwe urovere rutsoka rwako pabwe.
\v	13	Uchatsika pamusoro peshumba nechiva; mwana weshumba nebukanana uchatsikira pasi.
\p
\v	14	Nokuti wakandida zvikuru, naizvozvo ndichamununura. Ndichamuisa pakakwirira, nokuti wakaziva zita rangu.
\v	15	Achadana kwandiri, uye ndichamupindura; ndinaye padambudziko; ndichamununura, uye ndichamukudza.
\v	16	Ndichamugutsa nekureba kwemazuva, uye ndichamutaridza ruponeso rwangu.
\c	92
\s	Rwiyo rwekurumbidza Jehovha
\p
\v	1	Zvakanakakuvonga Jehovha, nekuimbira zita renyu rumbidzo, imwi Wekumusoro-soro.
\v	2	Kuparidzarudo rweunyoro hwenyu mangwanani, nekutendeka kwenyu usiku hwose.
\v	3	Pachiridzwachehungiso gumi, nepamutengeranwa, nembira inorira zvakanaka.
\v	4	Nokutiimwi Jehovha, makandifadza nebasa renyu; ndichaimba maererano nemabasa emaoko enyu.
\v	5	Jehovha,akakura sei mabasa enyu! Ndangariro dzenyu dzakadzika kwazvo.
\v	6	Chitutahachizivi; nebenzi harinzwisisi izvi.
\v	7	Kanavakaipa vachimera seuswa, uye vaiti vose vezvakaipa vachitunga; kuti vaparadzwe nekusingaperi.
\p
\v	8	Asiimwi Jehovha makakwirira kusvika rinhi narinhi.
\v	9	Nokutitarirai, vavengi venyu, Jehovha, nokuti tarirai, vavengi venyu vachaparara; vose vaiti vezvakaipa vachaparadzirwa.
\v	10	Asi muchasimudza runyanga rwangu serwenyati; ndakazodzwa nemafuta matsva.
\v	11	Ziso ranguwo richaona  chishuwo changu pavavengi vangu, nzeve dzangu dzichanzwa  zvakaitirwa vaiti vezvakaipa vakandimukira.
\v	12	Wakarurama achatunga semuchindwe; achakura semusidhari paRebhanoni.
\v	13	Vakasimwa mumba maJehovha, vachatunga muvazhe dzaMwari wedu.
\v	14	Vacharamba vachibereka zvibereko pakukwegura; vachava vakakora nevatsva;
\v	15	kuparidza kuti Jehovha wakarurama; idombo rangu, uye hakuna kusarurama kwaari.
\c	93
\s	Umambo hwaJehovha
\p
\v	1	Jehovhaanotonga; wakapfekedzwa umambo; Jehovha wakapfekedzwa simba; wakazvisunga chiuno. Nenyika yakasimbiswa; haingazungunuswi.
\v	2	Chigarochenyu cheushe chakasimbiswa kare; imwi  muripo kubva pakusingaperi.
\p
\v	3	Nzizidzakasimudza, Jehovha; nzizi dzakasimudza inzwi radzo; nzizi dzakasimudza kutinhira kwadzo.
\v	4	Jehovhawakakwirira ane simba kupfuura kutinhira kwemvura zhinji,  nemafungu ane simba egungwa.
\p
\v	5	Zvipupurirozvenyu ndezvechokwadi kwazvo; utsvene hwakafanira imba yenyu, Jehovha, kusvika pakureba kwemazuva.
\c	94
\s	Jehovha ndiye Mutsivi
\p
\v	1	Mwariwetsivo zhinji, Jehovha, Mwari wetsivo zhinji, penyai.
\v	2	Simukirai,Mutongi wenyika; tsivai mubairo kune vanozvikudza.
\p
\v	3	Kusvikarinhi vakaipa, Jehovha, kusvika rinhi vakaipa vachipembera?
\v	4	Vanodurura mashoko, vanotaura vakasimba, vose vaiti vezvakaipa vachizvikudza.
\v	5	Vanopwanyavanhu venyu, Jehovha, nekutambudza nhaka yenyu.
\v	6	Vanourayachirikadzi nemutorwa, nenherera vanodziponda.
\v	7	Zvakadarovanoti: Jehovha haaoni, naMwari waJakove haazvicherekedzi.
\p
\v	8	Nzwisisaiimwi matununu pakati pevanhu; nemwi mapenzi, muchachenjera rinhi?
\v	9	Iyewakasima nzeve haanzwi here? Iye wakaumba ziso haaoni here?
\v	10	Iye anoraira vahedheni haarangi here? Iye anodzidzisa munhu ruzivo  haazivi here?
\v	11	Jehovha anoziva ndangariro dzemunhu, kuti hadzina maturo.
\v	12	Wakaropafadzwa murume wamunoranga, Jehovha, nekumudzidzisa kubva mumurau wenyu.
\v	13	Kumuzorodza pamazuva ezvakaipa, kusvika kwachererwa wakaipa gomba.
\v	14	Nokuti Jehovha haangarasi vanhu vake; nenhaka yake haasii.
\v	15	Nokuti mutongo uchadzokera kukururama; nevose vakarurama pamoyo vachautevera.
\p
\v	16	Ndiani achandisimukira kurwisa vaiti vezvakaipa? Ndiani achandimirira kurwisa vabati vezvakaipa?
\v	17	Dai Jehovha aisava rubatsiro rwangu, mweya weupenyu wangu ungadai nepadiki wakagara pakuti zii.
\v	18	Pandakati: Rutsoka rwangu rwotedzemuka: Tsitsi dzenyu, Jehovha, dzakanditsigira.
\v	19	Muuwandu hwendangariro dzangu mukati mangu nyaradzo dzenyu dzakafadza mweya weupenyu wangu.
\v	20	Chigaro cheushe chezvakaipa chingadyidzana nemwi here, chinoumba dambudziko nemurau here?
\p
\v	21	Vanounganira kurwisa mweya weupenyu wewakarurama, nekupa mhosva ropa risina mhosva.
\v	22	Asi Jehovha inhare yangu; naMwari wangu idombo reutiziro hwangu.
\v	23	Zvino achadzosera pamusoro pavo chitadzo chavo. Uye avapedze pakuipa kwavo. Jehovha Mwari wedu achavapedza.
\c	95
\s	Jehovha ngaakudzwe ateererwe nevanhu
\p
\v	1	Uyai,tiimbire Jehovha; tipururudzire dombo reruponeso rwedu.
\v	2	Ngatiuyepamberi pake nekuvonga, timupururudzire nemapisarema.
\p
\v	3	NokutiJehovha ndiMwari mukuru, naMambo mukuru pamusoro pevamwari vose.
\v	4	Muruokorwaiye mune nzvimbo dzepanyika dzakadzika, nenhongonya dzemakomo ndedzake.
\v	5	Uyogungwa riri rake, nokuti ndiye wakariita; uye maoko ake akaumba panyika pakaoma.
\p
\v	6	Uyai,tinamate tikotamire pasi; ngatifugame pamberi paJehovha muiti wedu.
\v	7	Nokutiiye ndiMwari wedu, nesu tiri vanhu vemafuro ake nemakwai eruoko rwake.
\p	Nhasi dai muchinzwa inzwi rake,
\v	8	musaomesamoyo yenyu sepakupikisana, sezuva remuedzo murenje.
\v	9	Madzibabaenyu paakandiedza vachindiidza, hongu vakaona basa rangu.
\v	10	Makore makumi mana ndakasemeswa nezera  iro, kusvika ndati: Ivo vanhu vanotsauka mumoyo; uye ivo havazivi nzira dzangu.
\v	11	Naizvozvo vandakapikira pakutsamwa kwangu  ndikati: Havangatongopindi muzororo rangu.
\c	96
\s	Jehovha ndiMambo
\p
\v	1	ImbiraiJehovha rwiyo rutsva; imbirai Jehovha, pasi pose.
\v	2	ImbiraiJehovha; rumbidzai zita rake; paridzai ruponeso rwake kubva pazuva kusvika pazuva.
\v	3	Rondedzeraikubwinya kwake pakati pevahedheni, zvishamiso zvake pakati pevanhu vose.
\v	4	NokutiJehovha mukuru, uye anofanira kurumbidzwa zvikuru; iye anotyisa pamusoro pavamwari vose.
\v	5	Nokutivamwari vose vendudzi zvifananidzo; asi Jehovha wakaita matenga.
\v	6	Rukudzonekubwinya zviri pamberi pake; simba nekunaka zviri muimba yake tsvene.
\v	7	Ipaikuna Jehovha, imwi mazera emarudzi, ipai kuna Jehovha rumbidzo nesimba.
\p
\v	8	Ipaikuna Jehovha rumbidzo yezita rake; unzai chipo, mupinde pavazhe dzake.
\v	9	NamataiJehovha mukunaka kweutsvene; mudedere pamberi pake, pasi pose.
\v	10	Itiyi pakati pevahedheni: Jehovha anotonga; nenyika ichasimbiswa, isazungunuswa; achatonga vanhu mukururama kukuru.
\p
\v	11	Matenga ngaafare, nenyika ngaifarisise; gungwa ngaritinhire nekuzara kwaro.
\v	12	Sango ngarifare, nezvose zviri mariri; ipapo miti yose yedondo ichaimba nemufaro.
\v	13	Pamberi paJehovha, nokuti anouya, nokuti anouya kuzotonga pasi; achatonga nyika nekururama, nevanhu nekutendeka kwake.
\c	97
\s	Ukuru hwaJehovha Mambo
\p
\v	1	Jehovhaanotonga; nyika ngaifare; zviwi zvizhinji ngazvipembere.
\v	2	Makorenerima zvinomukomberedza; kururama nemutongo ugaro hwechigaro chake cheushe.
\v	3	Motounotungamira pamberi pake, uye unopisa vavengi vake mativi ose.
\v	4	Mhenidzake dzakavheneka nyika; pasi pakaona ndokudedera.
\v	5	Makomoakanyunguduka senamo pamberi paJehovha, pamberi paShe wepasi pose.
\v	6	Matengaanodudzira kururama kwake; nevanhu vose vanoona kubwinya kwake.
\v	7	Vanonyaravose vanoshumira mifananidzo yakavezwa, vanozvikudza nezvimwari; mushumirei imwi mose vamwari.
\p
\v	8	Ziyonirakanzwa ndokufara, nevakunda vaJudha vakapembera, nekuda kwemitongo yenyu, Jehovha.
\v	9	Nokutiimwi Jehovha, makakwirira pamusoro penyika yose; makakwiridzwa kwazvo pamusoro pevamwari vose.
\p
\v	10	Imwi vanoda Jehovha, vengai zvakaipa; anochengetedza mweya yeupenyu yevatsvene vake; avanunure muruoko rwevakaipa.
\v	11	Chiedza chinodzvarirwa wakarurama, nemufaro vane moyo yakarurama.
\v	12	Farai muna Jehovha, imwi vakarurama, uye vongai pakurangarira utsvene hwake.
\c	98
\s	Jehovha mutongi wepanyika
\p
\v	1	ImbiraiJehovha rwiyo rutsva; nokuti wakaita zvinhu zvinoshamisa; ruoko rwake rwerudyi, nechanza chake chitsvene, zvakamuwanira kukunda.
\v	2	Jehovhawakazivisa ruponeso rwake; wakazarura pachena kururama kwake pameso pevahedheni.
\v	3	Wakarangariratsitsi dzake nekutendeka kwake kuimba yaIsraeri; migumo yose yenyika yakaona ruponeso rwaMwari wedu.
\p
\v	4	PururudziraiJehovha, imwi pasi pose; mudanidzire zvikuru, mufare, muimbe rumbidzo.
\v	5	ImbiraiJehovha nembira, nembira uye nenzwi rekuimba,
\v	6	nehwamandazhinji, neinzwi renyanga yegondohwe; pururudzai pamberi paMambo Jehovha.
\v	7	Gungwangariombe nekuzara kwaro, nyika nevagere mairi.
\v	8	Nzizingadziombere maoko, makomo ngaaimbe pamwe nemufaro.
\v	9	PamberipaJehovha, nokuti anouya kuzotonga pasi; achatonga nyika zvakarurama, nemarudzi nekururama kukuru.
\c	99
\s	Jehovha anotonga
\p
\v	1	Jehovhaanotonga; vanhu ngavadedere; mugari wepamakerubhi; nyika ngaizununguke.
\v	2	Jehovhamukuru muZiyoni; uye wakakwirira pamusoro pevanhu vose.
\v	3	Ngavarumbidzezita renyu guru uye rinotyisa; iye mutsvene.
\p
\v	4	Simbaramambo rinodawo mutongo; imwi munosimbisa kururama kukuru; imwi munoita mutongo nekururama muna Jakove.
\v	5	KwiridziraiJehovha Mwari wedu, uye namatai pachitsiko chetsoka dzake; iye mutsvene.
\p
\v	6	MozisinaAroni pakati pevapristi vake, naSamueri pakati pevanodana zita rake; vakadana kuna Jehovha, iye ndokuvapindura.
\v	7	Wakatauranavo mukati meshongwe yegore; vakachengeta zvipupuriro zvake nemurairo waakavapa.
\v	8	JehovhaMwari wedu, imwi makavapindura; maiva Mwari waivakanganwira, kunyange muchitsiva pazviito zvavo.
\p
\v	9	KwiridziraiJehovha Mwari wedu, uye namatai pagomo rake dzvene; nokuti Jehovha Mwari wedu mutsvene.
